Adare, sAgaNike embudaralli I pratyaya aN (illavE aNe) embu
dara munde ike emba rUpadalli bandide. dabbALike embudaralli I
pratyayadondige ALe emba pratyaya bandiruva hAge kANisuttade.

mEle koTTiruva nAmapadagaLannu kriyApadavondakke eraDu bEre
bEre pratyayagaLannu sErisi tayArisalAgideyendu hELuva badalu aLi
illavE aN emba pratyayagaLa baLakeyinda tayArAda nAmapadagaLige
ike-ige pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisalAgideyendU hELalu sAdhya
vide. huTTuvaLi, sAguvaLi modalAda padagaLalli vaLi emba
pratyayada mUlaka, mattu sAgaNe, tirugaNe modalAda padagaLalli
aNe emba pratyayada mUlaka intaha nAmapadagaLannu
tayArisalAgide.

ondu vyavasAya illavE guNadharmavannAdharisi vyaktigaLannu
hesarisuvantaha (illavE antaha guNadharmavannE sUcisuvantaha)
kelavu SabdagaLige ike emba pratyayavondannu sErisi A vyavasAya
illavE guNadharmavannu hesarisuvantaha nAmapadavannu tayArisalu


sAdhyavide. intaha SabdagaLu nEravAgi samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandu
virabahudu, illavE kannaDada SabdagaLige gAra (illavE vanta) emba
pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisidavugaLirabahudu. udA:

madhyastha madhyasthike billugAra billugArike
SrImanta SrImantike mInugAra mInugArike
unnata unnatike maDivanta
maDivantike

mAsTarik emba padadalli I pratyaya ingliSh‌ninda eravalAgi
bandiruva mAsTar emba padadondige bandide.

intaha padagaLalli baruva ike emba pratyaya mEle vivarisiruva
ike-ige pratyayakke sambandhisidudE athavA samskxtadinda eravalAgi
bandiruva bEre kelavu padagaLalli kANisuva ika emba innondu
pratyayakke (udA: kShaNa-kShaNika, yantra-yAntrika ityAdi (vivaragaLige
೮.೩.೫ nODi)) sambandhisidudE emba viShayadalli ondu nirdhArakke
baruvudu svalpa kaShTa.

## (pha) ike emba padarUpa pratyaya

mEle koTTiruva ike-ige emba pratyayadinda bhinnavAgiruva mattu
ellA sandarbhagaLallU ike emba ondE rUpadalliruva padarUpa
pratyayavondu kannaDadalli baLakeyallide. idannu kriyApadagaLige sErisi
avugaLa kriyArUpavondannu tayArisalu sAdhyavide. idu kriyApada
gaLu nirdESisuva ghaTanegaLannu varNisuttadallade hesarisuvudilla.
udA:

anju anjuvike bare bareyuvike
mADu mADuvike kuDi kuDiyuvike
hogaLu hogaLuvike iru iruvike
bayasu bayasuvike tappu tappuvike

I pratyayavannu sErisidAga ukArAnta kriyApadagaLa koneyalli
vakAra sErikoLLuttade, mattu ikArAnta mattu ekArAnta kriyApada


gaLa koneyalli vakAra mAtravallade ya emba akSharavU sErikoLLuttade
embudannu mElina udAharaNegaLinda tiLiyabahudu.

ike emba I pratyayavannoLagonDiruva kriyArUpagaLannu nAma
padagaLa sthAnadalli baLasalu sAdhyaviddu, ivakke bEre bEre vibhakti
pratyayagaLannU sErisalu sAdhyavide. udA:

1. (೧ka) Akeya hADuvikeyannu ellarU hogaLuttiddAre.
2. (೧kha) nimma hogaLuvikeyinda avanu ubbihOgiddAne.
3. (೧ga) avaLa aLuvikege kallU karagItu.

1. (i) kelavu vyatyAsagaLu
2. kriyApadagaLinda kriyArUpagaLannu tayArisalu baLasuva I ike emba
3. pratyaya padarUpa pratyayavallade padapratyayavalla. adu mEle
4. vivarisiruva ike-ige emba padapratyayakkinta tIra bhinnavAdudu. pada
5. pratyayagaLigU mattu padarUpa pratyayagaLigU naDuve entaha vyatyAsa
6. gaLella kANisaballuvu embudannu mEle ೧.೬ralli vivarisalAgide.
7. intaha vyatyAsagaLu I ike-ige mattu ike emba eraDu pratyayagaLa
8. naDuveyU kANisuvuvembudannu avugaLa naDuviruva keLagina vyatyAsa
9. gaLu spaShTapaDisuttave.
10. (೧) ike emba padarUpa pratyaya ellA kriyApadagaLondigU
11. baraballudu. I viShayadalli ondU apavAdavilla. samskxtadinda
12. eravalAgi bandiruva mattu isu emba pratyayada mUlaka kannaDadalli
13. kriyApadavAgi baLakeyAguva padagaLondigU idu baraballudembu
14. dannu keLagina udAharaNegaLalli kANabahudu.
16. anumatisu anumatisuvike
17. SikShisu SikShisuvike
18. virOdhisu virOdhisuvike
19. rakShisu rakShisuvike
21. idakke vyatiriktavAgi, ike-ige emba padapratyayada baLake kelavE
22. kelavu kriyApadagaLondige mAtra rUDhiyallide. udAharaNegAgi, bare,
23. kuDi, mADu, duDuku, tirugu modalAda halavAru kriyApada
24. gaLondige I pratyayada baLake rUDhiyallilla. ike emba padarUpa


pratyayavannu ivellavakkU sErisi hELalu sAdhyavide. idallade, samskxta
dinda eravalAgi bandiruva anumatisu, SikShisu modalAda kriyApada
gaLondige ike emba padarUpa pratyayavannu sErisi hELuva hAge
ike-ige emba padapratyayavannu sErisi hELalu sAdhyavAgadu.

(೨) ike emba padarUpa pratyayada baLakeyalli ike-ige emba
padapratyayada baLakeyalli kANisuvantaha aniyamita badalAvaNega
LAvuvU kANisuvudilla. ellA rItiya kriyApadagaLondigU adu
ike emba ondE rUpadalli baruttade. mEle sUcisidante, ukArada
anantara vakAra sErikoLLuvudu mattu ekAra hAgU ikAragaLa
anantara yav embudu sErikoLLuvudu emba eraDu sandhiniyama
gaLu mAtra ivugaLa baLakeyalli kANisuva badalAvaNegaLu. I eraDu
badalAvaNegaLu ellA sandarbhagaLallU niyamitavAgi baruttiddu, avakke
yAva apavAdavU illa.

kriyApadagaLU kUDa, ike emba padarUpa pratyayadondige
svalpavU badalAvaNeyillade sErikoLLuttave. udAharaNegAgi, kriyApada
gaLa koneyalli baruva su emba pratyaya illavE u emba svara I
pratyaya sEridAga biddu hOguvudilla, mattu kriyApadagaLa kone
yalli baruva ekAra akAravAgi illavE ukAravAgi badalAguvudilla.
ike-ige emba padapratyayakkU mattu ike emba padarUpa pratyayakkU
naDuviruva I vyatyAsavannu keLage koTTiruva udAharaNegaLalli kANa
bahudu.

(೩) arthada maTTigU I eraDu pratyayagaLa naDuve vyatyAsavide.
mEleyE vivarisidante, ike-ige pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisida
nAmapadagaLige avugaLa oLaracaneya AdhArada mEle niyamitavAgi
artha hELalu sAdhyavAgadu. avellavakkU oLaracane ondE rItiya
dAdarU artha mAtra aniyamitavAgi bEre bErAgiruttade. Adare,
ike emba padarUpa pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisida ellA kriyArUpa
gaLigU ondE rItiya arthavide. avella varNisuva vidhAnada mUlaka
avugaLalli bandiruva kriyApadavu nirdESisuva ghaTaneyannu gurutisu
ttave.

bayasu bayake bayasuvike

kettu kettige kettuvike

hAsu hAsuge hAsuvike

hiDi hiDike hiDiyuvike

moLe moLake moLeyuvike

holi holige holiyuvike

I ellA vyatyAsagaLa AdhArada mEle ike embudu kriyA
padagaLinda kriyArUpagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi baLasuva padarUpa
pratyayavendU mattu ike-ige embudu prAmukhyavAgi kriyApada
gaLinda nAmapadagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi baLasuva adakkinta tIra
bhinnavAda padapratyayavendU hELabEkAguttade.


<a id="sec-4-3-2"></a>

## ೪.೩.೨ ta-tE pratyaya

ikAra mattu ekAragaLalli konegoLLuva kriyApadagaLige ta illavE te
emba rUpadalliruva I pratyayavannu sErisi kelavu nAmapadagaLannu
tayArisalu sAdhyavide. I eraDu rUpagaLalli te embudara baLake
gintalU ta embudara baLakeyE jAsti. Adare ivugaLalli yAvudannu
elli baLasabEku emba viShayadalli niyamavEnU iruva hAge
kANisuvudilla. te embudarondige bandAga kriyApadagaLa koneya
ekAra akAravAguttade (udA: naDe-naDate), Adare ta embuda
rondige bandAga adu hAgeyE badalAgade uLiyuttade (udA:
hoDe-hoDeta).


I pratyayada mUlaka tayArAda nAmapadagaLu sAmAnyavAgi
kriyApadavu nirdESisuva ghaTaneyannu illavE adarinda siddhavAguva
guNadharmavannu hesarisuttave. udA:

aniyamitavAgi intaha nAmapadagaLu kriyApadavu nirdESisuva
ghaTaneyalli baruva vastu, prANi modalAduvannu hesarisuttiralU
sAdhyavide (udA: miDi-miDite). tappu-tappita embudaralli I
pratyaya ukAradalli konegoLLuva kriyApadadondigU bandiruva hAge
kANisuttade.

samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva kelavu nAmapadagaLalli te
emba pratyayavondu kANisuttade. udA:

adhyakSha adhyakShate
arha arhate
kavi kavite
dakSha dakShate

Adare I te emba pratyayavannu nAmapadagaLigallade kriyApadagaLige
sErisuvudilla. vyaktiyobbanannu hesarisuva nAmapadadinda A vyaktiya
guNadharmavannu hesarisuva bErondu nAmapadavannu sAdhisalu I
pratyayada baLakeyAguttade. idu samskxtada tA emba pratyayada kannaDa
rUpa. mEle vivarisiruva ta-te idakkinta bhinnavAdudu.



<a id="sec-4-3-3"></a>

## ೪.೩.೩ A pratyaya

idu mukhyavAgi gu illavE Du emba akSharagaLalli konegoLLuva
kriyApadagaLinda nAmapadagaLannu tayArisuvalli baLakeyAguttade. I
pratyaya sEridAga kriyApadagaLa koneyalliruva gu mattu Du emba
akSharagaLu k mattu T endAguttave (endare, gakAra, DakAragaLu
kakAra, TakAragaLAguttave mattu avugaLa anantara baruva ukAra
bidduhOguttade).

ADu embudaralli konegoLLuva halavu 'kUDu'kriyApadagaLu
kannaDadalliddu avugaLalli kelavu kriyApadagaLondige I pratyaya bara
balludu. intaha baLakeyallU kriyApadada koneya Du emba akShara
T endAguttade. udA:

hOrADu hOrATa

tirugADu tirugATa

ODADu ODATa

baddADu baddATa

Adare I pratyaya intaha ellA kUDukriyApadagagaLondigU
niyamitavAgi baruvudilla. udAharaNegAgi, bisADu, nagADu, mAta
nADu modalAdavugaLondige idu baruvudilla, mattu I pratyayava
nnoLagonDiruva mArATa, huDugATa modalAda bEre kelavu
nAmapadagaLige samanAda kUDukriyApada kannaDadalli baLakeyallilla.
idallade, taletiruka, dArihOka modalAda bEre kelavu nAmapada
gaLalli I pratyaya bandiruva hAge kANisuttade, Adare ivannu
tayArisalu bEkAguva kUDukriyApadagaLu kannaDadalli baLakeyallilla.


Udu emba kriyApadakke idE pratyayavannu sErisi Uta emba
padavannu tayArisiruvalli dakAra takAravAgiruvudannu kANabahudu.

I pratyayada mUlaka tayArAguva nAmapadagaLa arthavU
aniyamitavAdudu. heccineDegaLallU idu kriyApadavu nirdESisuva
ghaTaneyannu hesarisuttade (udA: naDugu-naDuka, marugu-maruka).
Adare, kelaveDegaLalli ondu viSiShTavAda ghaTaneyannu mAtravE hesarisu
ttade (udA: mADu-mATa), mattu bEre kelavu kaDegaLalli antaha
ghaTaneyannu naDesuva vyaktiyannu hesarisuttade (udA: tirugu-tiruka).

agalu-agali mattu tIru-tIra embavugaLalli idE pratyaya ru
mattu lu emba akSharagaLalli konegoLLuva kriyApadagaLondige
bandiruvudannu kANabahudu.

gaLalli heccinavU I pratyaya sEridAga avugaLa koneyalli baruva
ekAravannu akAravAgi badalAyisuttave. udA:

vannU mattu tiruvu embudu ghaTaneya sthAnavannU hesarisuttave.


<a id="sec-4-3-5"></a>

## ೪.೩.೫ vaLi pratyaya

kriyApadagaLige I pratyayavannu sErisidAga, avugaLa koneyalli baruva
ekAra akAravAguttade, mattu ikAra ukAravAguttade. Adare ukAra
mAtra badalAgade hAgeyE uLiyuttade. idallade, udA:

</tr>

tiLuvaLike mattu naDavaLike emba eraDu padagaLalli I pratyaya ke
emba innondu pratyayadondige bandide. mattu ADaLita emba
padadalli ta emba pratyayadondige bandide. idallade, ADaLita emba


padadalli kriyApadadallidda LakAra DakAravAgide, mattu vaLi pratyayada
vakAra biddu hOgide.

gottu emba AkhyAta padadondigU I pratyaya bandiruvudannu
gottuvaLi emba nAmapadadalli kANabahudu. dabbALike
embudarallU idE pratyaya (dabbu emba kriyApadadondige)
bandiralu sAdhyaviddu, illi idakke ALi emba rUpavide.

aLi emba rUpadalliruva pratyayavondu AkaLisu, appaLisu,
kuppaLisu, bikkaLisu modalAda kelavu kriyApadagaLalli baruvudembu
dannu munde AranE adhyAyadalli nODaliruvevu. adu I pratyayakke
sambandhisiralu sAdhyavide. idE pratyaya heggaLike emba padadalli hiri
emba guNapadada heg emba rUpadondige bandide.


<a id="sec-4-3-6"></a>

## ೪.೩.೬ vaN pratyaya

I pratyaya adara ellA baLakegaLallU mEle ೪.೩.೧ralli vivarisida
ike-ige pratyayada ige emba rUpadondige baruttade. kriyApadada
koneya ekAra I pratyaya sEridAga akAravAguttade mattu ukAra
biddu hOguttade. ukAradalli konegoLLuva kriyApadadondige idu
aN emba rUpadalli baruttade.

maduvaNiga emba nAmapadadalli I pratyaya kriyApadadondige
baruva badalu maduve emba bErondu nAmapadadondige (mattu
iga emba pratyayadondige) bandiruvudannu kANabahudu.

tirugaNe, sAgaNe mattu badalAvaNe emba padagaLalli kANisuva
aNe emba pratyaya mattu hondANike, sAgANike, tiddANike
modalAda padagaLalli kANisuva AN emba pratyaya - ivugaLU I
pratyayakke sambandhisidavugaLAgiralu sAdhyavide.

dAga kriyApadagaLa koneya ukAra biddu hOguttade. Adare bALu
emba kriyApadadalli mAtra, adu vakAravAgi badalAguttade. idallade,
kollu emba kriyApadadalli baruva ottakSharadinda ondu vyanjanavU
biddu hOguttade. udA:

sEridAga kriyApadagaLa koneyalli baruva ukAra biddu hOguttade.

<a id="sec-4-3-10"></a>

## ೪.೩.೧೦ 'sonne' pratyaya

kannaDadalli kelavu padagaLannu avugaLalli yAva badalAvaNeyannU
mADade nAmapadagaLannAgi illavE kriyApadagaLannAgi baLasalu sAdhya
vide. udAharaNegAgi, keLage koTTiruva (೨ka-ga) vAkyagaLannu gamanisa
bahudu.

1. (೨ka) avaLu ondu hADannu hADidaLu.
2. (೨kha) guDugu guDugitu, mincu mincitu.
3. (೨ga) avanu kaTTida kaTTu saDilAgide.

(೨ka)dalli hADu emba pada eraDu bAri bandiddu, modalaneya baLake
yalli adu nAmapadavAgiyU mattu eraDaneya baLakeyalli kriyApada
vAgiyU bandide. idE rItiyalli (೨kha)dalli guDugu mattu
mincu emba padagaLu mattu (೨ga)dalli kaTTu emba pada yAva
rItiya badalAvaNegU oLagAgade nAmapada mattu kriyApadagaLAgi
bandiru vudannu kANabahudu.

intaha padagaLu mUladalli kriyApadagaLendU, mattu
avakkondu 'sonne' pratyayavannu sErisuvudara mUlaka avugaLinda
nAmapadagaLannu tayArisalAgideyendU hELuva kramavide. kannaDadalli


sAmAnyavAgi kriyApadagaLinda pratyayagaLannu sErisi nAmapadagaLannu
tayArisuvudE jAsti. isu emba pratyayavannu baLasi nAmapadagaLinda
kriyApadagaLannu tayArisalu sAdhyavideyEnO nija. Adare idakke
kannaDada nAmapada gaLigintalU samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda
nAmapadagaLannu baLasu vudE jAsti (೬.೪ nODi). idakkinta bhinnavAda
pratyayagaLu kannaDada kriyApadagaLalli cAritrika avaSEShagaLAgi mAtra
kANisikoLLuttave (೬.೩ nODi).

I viShayagaLa AdhArada mEle, nAmapada mattu kriyApadagaLa
naDuve sambandhaviruvallella kriyApadavE mUlavendU mattu nAma
pada kriyApadakke yAvudAdarondu pratyayavannu (illavE padavannu)
sErisuvudara mUlaka tayArAguvantahadendU vAdisalu sAdhyavide.

I rIti nAmapadagaLigU mattu kriyApadagaLigU ondE rUpa
viruvudannu I keLagina udAharaNegaLalli kANabahudu.

<table>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>ನಗು</td>
<td>ಓದು</td>
<td>ಮಿಂಚು</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ಅಳು</td>
<td>ಹಾಡು</td>
<td>ಗುಡುಗು</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ನುಡಿ</td>
<td>ಕೆಮ್ಮು</td>
<td>ಬೆವರು</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ಉರಿ</td>
<td>ತಪ್ಪು</td>
<td>ಬದುಕು</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ಬೆಳೆ</td>
<td>ಕಟ್ಟು</td>
<td>ಉಗುಳು</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ಕರೆ</td>
<td>ಗುದ್ದು</td>
<td>ಉರುಳು</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

intaha padagaLa prayOgadalli kriyApadagaLu niyamitavAgi ondu
ghaTaneyannu nirdESisuvuvAdare, nAmapadagaLu aniyamitavAgi bEre
bEre rItiya arthagaLannu koDuttave. udAharaNegAgi, Odu, aLu,
kemmu modalAda nAmapadagaLu adE rUpada kriyApadagaLu nirdE
Sisuva ghaTanegaLannu hesarisuvuvAdare, hADu, beLe, bevaru
modalAda nAmapadagaLu antaha ghaTanegaLinda doreyuva
phalitAmSavannu hesarisu ttave.

arthadalli aniyamitate mattu vayvidhyavannu nAvu sAmAnyavAgi
pratyayaviruva nAmapadagaLallE kANuvevAda kAraNa, intaha nAmapada
gaLalli kriyApadagaLondige ondu 'sonne' pratyaya bandideyemba
mElina vAdakke I nAmapadagaLa arthadalli kANisuva aniyamitate
yU ondu AdhAravAgaballudu.



<a id="sec-4-3-11"></a>

## ೪.೩.೧೧ bEre kelavu pratyayagaLu

mAtravE kANisikoLLuva bEreyU kelavu pratyayagaLu kannaDadalli
kriyApadagaLinda nAmapadagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi baLakeyAguttave.
ivannu bEre bErAgi varNisuva badalu paTTimADi hELuvudE sulabha
vAdudarinda antaha pratyayagaLiruva padagaLa paTTiyondannu keLage
koDalAgide.

<a id="sec-4-4"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#sec-4-4)

## ೪.೪ nAmapadagaLinda tayArAda nAmapadagaLu

kannaDadalli nAmapadagaLannu bEre nAmapadagaLige yAvudAdarondu
pratyayavannu sErisuvudara mUlakavU tayArisalu sAdhyavide. udA
haraNegAgi, gANiga emba nAmapadavannu gANa emba bErondu nAma
padakke iga pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisalAgide mattu mUguti emba
nAmapadavannu mUru emba bErondu nAmapadakke ti emba
pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisalAgide.

Adare kannaDadalli I rIti tayArisalAgiruva nAmapadagaLa sankhye
jAsti illa. sAmAnyavAgi nAmapadagaLannu bEre nAmapadagaLondige
illavE kriyApada athavA guNapadagaLondige sErisi jODupadagaLannu
tayArisuvudE kannaDadalli heccu baLakeyalliruva vidhAna. udAharaNe
gAgi, kay emba nAmapadavannu baLasi halavu oLaracaneyiruva nAma
padagaLannu tayArisalAgiddu, ivellavU jODupadagaLa rUpadalliruvu
dannu gamanisabahudu.

kaykoDali kaygUsu
kaygannaDi kaycIla
kaygADi kaycaLaka
kaygelasa kaypiDi
kaygUli kaybaraha
kaygaDa kaymagga, ityAdi


nAmapadagaLinda bEre nAmapadagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi baLasuva
pratyayagaLu kelavu kannaDadalli kANisuvuvAdarU, avugaLalli samskxta
dinda eravalAgi bandavugaLu illavE samskxtada pratyayagaLa mAdari
yalli siddhavAdavugaLE jAsti. udAharaNegAgi, samskxtada kx 'mADu'
emba kriyApadadinda siddhavAda kAra emba pratyaya (udA: citrakAra,
namaskAra, balAtkAra ityAdi) kannaDadalli gAra emba pratyayavAgi
halavu nAmapadagaLalli kANisikoLLuttade. udA:

idE rItiyalli, mEle ೪.೩.೧ralli vivarisida hAge, samskxtada
ike emba pratyayada mAdariyalli ondu vyavasAya illavE
guNadharma vannAdharisi vyaktigaLannu hesarisuva nAmapadagaLinda A
vyavasAya illavE guNadharmavannu hesarisuva nAmapadavannu
tayArisalu kannaDadalli ike emba pratyayada baLakeyAguttade.
kolegArike, billugArike, modalAda nAmapadagaLannu idakke
udAharaNegaLannAgi koDabahudu.

kannaDadavE Ada kelavu padagaLalli kANisuva strI-puruSha lingabhEda
vannu sUcisuva i mattu a emberaDu pratyayagaLigU (udA:
muduka-muduki) samskxtadinda kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva bEre
halavu padagaLalli kANisuva idE rUpada pratyayagaLu (udA: naTa-
naTi, lEkhaka-lEkhaki, SikShaka-SikShaki, ityAdi) mAdariyAgiralu sAdhya
vide. Adare, ukAradalli konegoLLuva halavu guNapadagaLindalU
vyavasthitavAgi I pratyayagaLannu baLasi nAmapadagaLannu tayArisalu
sAdhya embudannu munde ೪.೫ralli nODaliruvevu.

ganDu-heNNu emba arthabhEdavannu sUcisuva bEreyU kelavu
pratyayagaLu kannaDadallive. udAharaNegAgi, mEle koTTiruva gAra


emba pratyayadalli konegoLLuva nAmapadagaLalli kelavakke ti emba
pratyayavannu sErisi heNNu emba artha baruvante mADalu sAdhyavide.
udA:

baLegAra baLegArti
mAlegAra mAlegArti
edegAra edegArti
jotegAra jotegArti

vastu, viShaya, sthaLa modalAduvannu gurutisuva nAmapadagaLige
iga pratyayavannu sErisi, A vastu, viShaya, sthaLa modalAduvakke
sambandhisiruva vyaktigaLannu gurutisuva nAmapadagaLannu tayArisalu
sAdhyavide. udA:

vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLannu gurutisuva nAmapadagaLige tana
emba pratyayavannu sErisi, antaha vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa
svabhAvavannu gurutisuva nAmapadagaLannu tayArisabahudu. udA:

<td>ಜಾಣ</td>
<td>ಜಾಣತನ</td>
<td>ಮನೆ</td>
<td>ಮನೆತನ</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

I tana emba pratyaya guNapadagaLondigU baraballudembudannu
munde ೪.೫ralli nODaliruvevu.


idallade, onderaDu padagaLalli mAtravE kANisuvantaha bEre
kelavu pratyayagaLU kannaDadallive. ivugaLalli kelavannu keLage koTTiruva
paTTiyalli kANabahudu.

<a id="sec-4-5"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#sec-4-5)

## ೪.೫ guNapadagaLinda tayArAda nAmapadagaLu

guNapadagaLige kelavu pratyayagaLannu sErisuvudara mUlakavU kannaDadalli
nAmapadagaLannu tayArisalu sAdhyavide. idallade kelavu guNapadagaLu
pratyayagaLa sahAyavillade hAgeyE nEravAgi nAmapadagaLAgiyU bara
balluvu. (intaha guNapadagaLige ondu 'sonne'pratyayavannu sErisa
lAgideyendU hELalu sAdhyavide).


<a id="sec-4-5-1"></a>

## ೪.೫.೧ nEravAda baLake

kannaDadalli baruva guNapadagaLalli halavannu avugaLalli yAva badalA
vaNeyannU mADade nEravAgi nAmapadagaLa sthAnadalli baLasalu sAdhya
vide. udAharaNegAgi, kempu emba pada guNapadavAgiyU baLakeyAga
balludu mattu nAmapadavAgiyU baLakeyAgaballudu. udA:

(೩ka) I gODege kempu baNNa hAkiddu svalpa jAstiyAyitu.
(೩kha) I gODege kempu hAkiddu svalpa jAstiyAyitu.

(೩ka)dalli kempu embudu guNapadavAgi bandide mattu (೩kha)dalli
adE pada yAva badalAvaNeyU illade nAmapadavAgi bandide.


I rIti guNadharmavannu hesarisuva badalu antaha guNadharma
vannoLagonDiruva vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu hesarisuvudakkAgiyU
kelavu guNapadagaLu pratyayagaLa sahAyavillade nAmapadagaLAgi bara
balluvu. udA:

(೪ka) pArvatammanavaru ivattu ondu sihi tinDi mADiddare.
(೪kha) pArvatammanavaru ivattu ondu sihi mADiddAre.

(೪ka)dalli sihi embudu ondu guNapadavAgi bandide mattu (೪kha)
dalli adE pada ondu nAmapadavAgi bandide. Adare I eraDaneya
baLakeyalli adu sihi emba guNapadavu sUcisuva guNadharmavannu
hesarisuva badalu antaha guNadharmavannu paDediruva ondu vastuvannu
(sihiyAgiruva tinDiyannu) hesarisuttade.

huLi, gaTTi, daDDa, jANa modalAda guNapadagaLU idE
rItiyalli yAva badalAvaNeyU illade nAmapadagaLAgi guNadharma
vannu paDediruva vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu hesarisalu baraballuvu.

guNapadagaLannu avugaLa arthada AdhArada mEle aLate, prAya,
bele, baNNa, bhavtika guNadharma, mAnavIya guNadharma mattu vEga
embudAgi bEre bEre upavargagaLalli vingaDisalu sAdhyaviddu,
ivugaLalli modalaneya nAlku upavargagaLalli baruva padagaLu
mAdari guNapadagaLAgiruttave. uLida padagaLu kelavu viShayagaLalli
guNapadagaLa hAgiddare, bEre kelavu viShayagaLalli nAmapadagaLa
hAgiruttave. sAmAnyavAgi nAmapada mattu guNapadagaLemba eraDU
vargagaLalli baruva padagaLu intahavu.

mAdari guNapadagaLannu nAmapadagaLAgi baLasabEkiddalli avugaLalli
EnAdarU badalAvaNegaLannu mADikoLLabEkAguttade, illavE bEre
kelavu niyamagaLannu anusarisabEkAguttade. udAharaNegAgi, vyakti,
prANi, vastu modalAdavugaLa aLate illavE parimANavannu sUcisuva
guNapadagaLannu udda-giDDa, ettara-taggu, agala-sapura, dappa-teLu,
bhAra-hagura embantaha bEre bEre viruddhArthada jODigaLAgi sErisi
hELalu sAdhyavide.

intaha guNapadagaLa pratiyondu jODiyallU modalaneya
kAlannalli koTTiruva guNapadavannu mAtra nEravAgi ondu nAmapadada
sthAnadalli baLasalu sAdhyavide. idallade, A eraDu padagaLU oTTAgi


sUcisuva aLateyannu I ondE guNapada hesarisuttade. udAharaNe
gAgi keLage koTTiruva (೫ka-ga) vAkyagaLannu gamanisabahudu.

(Aka) A kOlu I kOliginta udda.

(೫೨) I kOlu A kOliginta giDDa.

(೫ga) A kOlina udda nAlkaDi, mattu I kOlina udda
mUraDi.

mEle (೫ka) vAkyadalli AkhyAtavAgi bandiruva udda emba guNapadakkU
mattu (೫kha) vAkyadalli bandiruva giDDa emba guNapadakkU pratiyAgi
(೫ga) vAkyadalli udda embudE nAmapadavAgi bandideyembudannu
gamanisabahudu. kOlu udda iddarU giDDa iddarU adara aLateyannu
sUcisalu udda emba padavannE nAmapadavAgi baLasabEkAguttade.

idE rItiyalli ettara mattu taggu emba guNapadagaLu sUcisuva
aLateyannu hesarisalu ettara emba padavE nAmapadavAgi baLake
yAguttade, mattu agali hAgU sapura emba guNapadagaLu sUcisuva
aLateyannu hesarisalu agali embudE nAmapadavAgi baLakeyAguttade.
mEle koTTiruva itara padagaLa baLakeyU intahadE embudannu
gamanisabahudu.


<a id="sec-4-5-2"></a>

## ೪.೫.೨ pratyayagaLa baLake

kuruDu, kivuDu, kuLLu, huccu modalAda manuShyaralli kANisuva
guNadharmagaLannu (adarallU prAmukhyavAgi korategaLannu) sUcisuva
kelavu guNapadagaLu sAmAnyavAgi ukAradalli konegoLLuttave. intaha
guNapadagaLige a 'ganDasu' mattu i 'hengasu' emba pratyayagaLa
llondannu sErisi nAmapadagaLannu tayArisalu sAdhyavide. I
pratyayagaLannu sErisidAga guNapadagaLa koneya ukAra biddu hOgu
ttade. udA:

sahAyavilladeyU nAmapadagaLAgi baraballuvAgiddu, antaha baLake
yalli avakke guNadharmaviruvavarannu hesarisuva badalu guNadharma
vannE hesarisuva arthaviruttade.

## (Taka) avanadu kuruDu buddhi.

## (Tavi) avana kivudige maddilla.

kelavu guNapadagaLige tana emba pratyayavannu sErisi, avu
sUcisuva guNadharmavannu hesarisalu sAdhyavide. udA:

I pratyaya padapratyayavE athavA padarUpa pratyayavE (endare
I pratyayaviruva padagaLu nAmapadagaLE athavA guNapadagaLa pada
rUpagaLE) emba viShayadalli sandEhavide. I pratyaya ellA rItiya
guNapadagaLondigU bAradiruvudu idannu padapratyayavendu hELalu
AdhAravAgaballudu. udAharaNegAgi, kappu illavE kempu emba
guNapadadondige I pratyaya baralAradu.

Adare idu baruvallella niyamitavAgi ondu guNadharmavannE
sUcisuva kAraNa, idu varNisuva vidhAnada mUlaka (೩.೧ nODi) A
guNadharmavannu gurutisuvudendu hELalu sAdhyavide. I viShayada
AdhArada mEle adannu guNapadada padarUpavendU hELalu sAdhyavide.


onderaDu nAmapadagaLalli mAtravE kANisuva bEre kelavu pratyaya
gaLU kannaDadalli guNapadagaLinda nAmapadagaLannu tayArisalu baLake
yallive. intaha padagaLa paTTiyannu keLage koDalAgide.

## ೪. sArAmSa

pratyayagaLannu baLasi tayArisida nAmapadagaLu kannaDadalli jAsti illa.
padagaLige pratyayagaLannu sErisuvudakkintalU bEre padagaLannE sErisi
jODupadagaLannu tayArisuvudE kannaDadalli heccu baLakeyalliruva
vidhAna. idallade, pratyayagaLannu baLasuvallU ondu padakke ondakkinta
jAsti pratyayagaLannu sErisi tayArisida padagaLu kannaDadalli bahaLa
kaDime.

pratyayagaLannu baLasi tayArisida nAmapadagaLalli kriyApadakke
pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisida nAmapadagaLE kannaDadalli jAsti. intaha
nAmapadagaLalli kANisuva pratyayagaLalli ike-ige embudE prAmukhya
vAdudu. nAmapada mattu guNapadagaLige pratyayagaLannu sErisi
tayArisida nAmapadagaLu kelavu kannaDadalli kANisuvuvAdarU intaha
padagaLa sankhye bahaLa kaDime. idallade, nAmapadagaLondige baruva pada


pratyayagaLalli heccinavU samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLalli
kANisuva pratyayagaLa mAdariyalli tayArAdavugaLa hAgive.


<a id="adhyAya-5"></a>

[English →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-en#chapter-5--compound-nouns) | [ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#adhyAya-5)

adhyAya aydu
jODupadagaLu


<a id="sec-5-1"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#sec-5-1)

## ೫.೧ gondalavannu hOgalADisuvudu

kESirAjana kAladindalU kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLalli samAsagaLa varNane
yembudu ondu doDDa gOjalumaya viShayavAgide. samskxta
samAsagaLa pariSIlaneya mUlaka kannaDa samAsagaLannu vivarisalu
yatnisiruvudu idakke ondu kAraNavAdare, jODupadagaLigU mattu
padagucchagaLigU naDuviruva vyatyAsavannu sariyAgi tiLidukoLLadiru
vudu innondu kAraNa. nAvu pariSIlisabEkAda vastu yAvudu
embudannE sariyAgi tiLidukoLLade spaShTavAgi arthavAguvantaha
varNaneyondannu koDalu sAdhyavilla tAne?

I gondalavannu hOgalADisalu nAvu mukhyavAgi mADa
bEkAda kelasagaLivu: hosagannaDadalli baruva samAsagaLentahavu embu
dannu tiLiyabEkiddare nAvu samskxtadalli baruva samAsagaLentahavu
embudannu tiLiyuva avaSyakateyilla. samskxtadinda kannaDakke eravalAgi
bandiruva padagaLa oLaracaneyantahadu embudannu tiLidukoLLuvalli
mAtra samskxta samAsagaLa tiLuvaLike sahAyakavAgaballudAdarU
alliyU adu atyavaSyavEnallavembudannu munde (೮.೩.೭ralli) nODa
liruvevu. hAgAgi, hosagannaDadalli baruva jODupadagaLa oLaracane
yannu varNisuvalli samskxtada samAsagaLannu gamanakke tegedukoLLa
diruvudE oLLeyadu.

idE rItiyalli, haLegannaDa illavE naDugannaDadalli mAtravE baLake
yalliruvantaha jODupadagaLa oLaracaneyannU hosagannaDadalli baruva
jODupadagaLannu varNisuvavaru gamanakke tegedukoLLabEkAgilla. kannaDa



bhASheyalli baruva padagaLa caritreyantahadu embudannu tiLiyubEkendi
ruvavaru mAtra I rIti haLegannaDa mattu naDugannaDa padagaLa oLaracane
yannu tiLiyuva avaSyakateyide.

samskxta vyAkaraNagaLalli baLakeyalliruva tatpuruSha, karmadhAraya,
dvigu, dvandva, bahuvrIhi modalAda pAribhAShika padagaLannE kannaDada
jODupadagaLannu (mattu avugaLa oLaracaneyalli kANisuva 'samAsa'
vemba hesarina vidhAnavannu) varNisuvudakkAgiyU baLasuvudu rUDhi.
Adare I padagaLu nammeduru samskxta samAsagaLannE tandirisuva
kAraNa, avannu baLasidalli kannaDa jODupadagaLa varNaneyalli samskxta
samAsagaLindAgiruva gondalavannu hOgalADisalu sAdhyavAgadu.

hAgAgi, I adhyAyadalli kannaDada jODupadagaLannu nEravAgi
kannaDadalli avakkiruva oLaracaneyantahadu embudannu pariSIlisuvudara
mUlaka varNisalAgide. haLegannaDa illavE naDugannaDadalli mAtravE
kANisuva jODupadagaLannu illi gamanisilla. samskxtada samAsagaLannU
I varNaneyalli pariSIlisilla. idallade, I varNaneyalli tatpuruSha,
karmadhAraya modalAda samskxtada pAribhAShika padagaLannU baLasilla.
kannaDada jODupadagaLannu nEravAgi A padagaLa oLaracaneyalli baruva
padagaLa sankhye, padavarga, avugaLa naDuve kANisuva sambandha moda
lAda viShayagaLannAdharisi varNisalAgide.

anantara bEreyE ondu vibhAgadalli (೫.೮ralli) ivattu kannaDada
vyAkaraNa pustakagaLalli kANisuva jODupadagaLa (mattu kannaDa samAsa
gaLa) varNanegaLu yAke iShTondu toDaku toDakAgive mattu kannaDada
jODupadagaLannu sariyAgi mattu spaShTavAgi tiLisikoDuvalli asamartha
vAgive embudannu vivarisalAgide. idallade, kannaDada jODupadagaLa
varNaneyalli samskxtada tatpuruSha, karmadhAraya modalAda pAri
bhAShika padagaLa baLake yAke samAdhAnakArakavalla embudannU vivarisa
lAgide.


<a id="sec-5-2"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#sec-5-2)

## ೫.೨ jODupadagaLu mattu padagucchagaLu

eraDu athavA jAsti padagaLannu oTTAgi jODisi ondE padavAgi
mADuva vidhAnakke samAsavendU mattu antaha vidhAnada mUlaka
tayArAda padavannu jODupadavendU kareyabahudu. udAharaNe
gAgi, keLaduTi embudu ondu jODupada. yAkendare, idaralli
keLage mattu tuTi emba eraDu padagaLannu oTTAgi jODisi bEreyE




ondu padavannu tayArisalAgide, mattu I padada mUlaka bAyalli
ruva eraDu tuTigaLalli keLaginadannu hesarisalAgide. kannaDadalli sAmAnya
vAgi intaha padagaLalli eraDu padagaLu mAtravE sEriruttaveyAda
kAraNa, jODupada emba I hesaru sUcisabahudAda 'eraDu' emba
arthadindalU kannaDada maTTige tondareyAguvudilla.

kannaDadalli yAva rItiya jODupadagaLella baLakeyallive mattu
avugaLa oLaracaneyantahadu embudannu vivarisi hELuvudE I
adhyAyada mukhya uddESa. I uddESavannu sariyAgi neravErisuvu
dakkAgi modalige jODupadagaLigU mattu kelavu viShayagaLalli
avugaLa hAgeyE kANisuva padagucchagaLigU naDuve entaha vyatyAsa
gaLive embudannu tiLiyuva avaSyakateyide. idallade, jODupada
gaLigU mattu hindina (nAlkanE) adhyAyadalli vivarisiruva pratyaya
viruva padagaLigU naDuve entaha vyatyAsavideyembudannU tiLidu
koLLuva avaSyakateyide.

jODupada mattu padagucchagaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsavannu tiLidu
koLLuvudu kannaDada maTTige ondu prAmukhyavAda kelasa. yAkendare,
kannaDada heccina vyAkaraNagaLallU I eraDu rItiya vAkyAmSagaLa naDu
viruva vyatyAsa aspaShTavAgiyE uLidide mAtravalla, kelaveDegaLalli
averaDU ondE emba bhAvaneyU baruvantide. udAharaNegAgi, A
mane, bALeya haNNu, Oduva huDuga modalAdavugaLalli gamaka,
tatpuruSha modalAda samAsagaLiveyembudAgi kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLalli
barediruvudannu kANabahudu.

Adare nijakkU A mane embudaralli A emba nirdESaka pada
dondige mane emba nAmapadavannu baLasalAgiddu, adondu
padaguccha vAgide. idE rItiyalli bALeya haNNu embudaralli eraDu
nAma padagaLannu a emba pratyayada mUlaka sambandhisalAgide, mattu
Oduva huDuga embudaralli Odu emba kriyApadavannu adara
sambandhaka kriyArUpada mUlaka huDuga emba nAmapadadondige
sambandhisalAgide. I mUru kaDegaLallU eraDeraDu padagaLu bandiddu,
avu padagucchagaLAgi uLidiveyallade ondE padavAgi oTTu sErilla.

jODupadagaLu eraDu athavA jAsti padagaLu oTTu sEri ondE
padavAguvudara mUlaka siddhavAda sanjYegaLallade padagucchagaLalla.
eraDu athavA jAsti padagaLu oTTige bandiveyAdarU ondE sanjYe
yAgade bEre bEre sanjYegaLAgi uLidiveyAdare adannu padagucchavennu




ttEve. jODupadagaLa racaneyalli padaracaneya niyamagaLu barutta
vAdare, padagucchagaLa racaneyalli vAkyaracaneya niyamagaLu baruttave.

udAharaNegAgi, keLaduTi emba jODupadavannu keLagina tuTi
emba padagucchadondige hOlisi nODabahudu. ivugaLalli modalane
yadannu tayArisuvalli keLage emba padada giDDarUpavAda keLa embu
dannu baLasalAgide mattu tuTi emba padadalli modalige baruva
takAravannu dakAravAgi badalAyisalAgide. kannaDadalli iveraDU pada
racaneyalli baruva badalAvaNeya niyamagaLu (೫.೭ nODi). idakke
badalu keLagina tuTi emba padagucchadalli I eraDu padagaLu
badalAgade uLidive mAtravalla, avugaLalli ondannu innondaroDane
sambandhisuvudakkAgi keLage emba padadondige a emba pratyayavannu
baLasalAgide. idu vAkyaracaneya niyamavallade padaracaneya niyama
valla.

jODupada mattu padagucchagaLa naDuve innondu prAmukhyavAda
vyatyAsavide. mEle mUraneya adhyAyadalli vivarisiruvante (೩.೩.೩
nODi), ondu nAmapadagucchada arthavEnembudannu nEravAgi adara
oLaracaneyannu pariSIlisuvudara mUlaka tiLidukoLLalu sAdhyavide.
Adare, ondu jODupadada arthavannu I rIti nEravAgi adara
oLaracaneya sahAyadinda tiLidukoLLalu sAdhyavAgadu. antaha pada
gurutisuva vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa guNadharmavEnu embudannu
tiLiyuvudara mUlakavEnE adara arthavEnendu hELalu sAdhya.
jODupadagaLa arthavannu avugaLa oLaracaneyinda Uhisalu
sAdhyavideyAdarU heccina sandarbhagaLallU antaha Uhe tappAgalu
sAdhyavide.

udAharaNegAgi, keLaduTi emba jODupadada oLaracaneyalli
keLagina tuTi emba nAmapadagucchavannu kANuvevAdarU 'keLagina tuTi'
gaLella keLaduTigaLAgirabEkAgilla. eraDu tuTigaLa ondu citradalli
keLaginadu keLagina tuTiyAgideyAdarU keLaduTiyAgilladiralu sAdhya
vide. yAkendare A citradalli ondara keLage ondAgi citrisiruva
tuTigaLeraDU mElduTiya citragaLAgiralu sAdhyavide. idallade,
innondu citradalli keLaduTiyannu mEle mattu mElduTiyannu adara
keLage citrisiralu sAdhyavideyAda kAraNa, adaralli 'mElina tuTi'yE
keLaduTiyAgiralu sAdhyavide.




keLaduTi emba pada obba vyaktiya (illavE prANiya) mukha
dalliruva eraDu tuTigaLalli keLaginadannu hesarisuttade. idu I jODu
padakke namma bhASheyalli rUDhavAgi bandiruvantaha baLake. I baLakeya
prakAra, mukhadalli keLagiruva tuTiya guNadharmagaLu yAvuvO
avugaLa AdhArada mEle mAtra keLaduTi emba I jODupadada
arthavannu nirdharisi hELabEkAguttade. A padada oLaracaneyalli baruva
keLa mattu tuTi emba padagaLa arthadinda nEravAgi adara arthavannu
paDeyalu sAdhyavAgadu.

jODupada mattu padagucchagaLa naDuve I rIti bahaLa mukhyavAda
mattu spaShTavAda vyatyAsagaLiveyAdarU, kelavondu sandarbhagaLalli
avugaLannu bErpaDisi hELuvudu svalpa kaShTavendE tOralu sAdhyavide.
idakke kAraNavEnendare, nammeduriruva ondu vAkyAmSa jODupadavE
athavA padagucchavE embudannu bariya A vAkyAmSavannu mAtra nODi
nirdharisalu baruvudilla. vAkyadalli adara baLakeyantahadu, adannu
baLasiruva vyaktiya ASayavEnu embudannU gamanisikoLLuvudu avaSya.
udAharaNegAgi, nAvu mEle mUranE adhyAyadalli (೩.೪ralli)
nODiruvante, bisinIru emba vAkyAmSa kelavondu sandarbhagaLalli
(udA: ADuganu snAna mADabEkendiruvAga) padagucchavAgiyU
mattu bEre kelavu sandarbhagaLalli (udA: ADuganu UTakke
kuLitiruvAga) jODupadavAgiyU baLakeyAgiralu sAdhyavide.
modalaneya baLake yalli adara arthavannu adara angagaLAgiruva bisi
mattu nIru emba eraDu padagaLa arthadinda paDeyalu sAdhyavide,
Adare eraDaneya baLakeyalli idu sAdhyavAgadu.

Adare idu bhASheya itara padagaLa illavE vAkyAmSagaLa baLake
yallU kANisuva vaySiShTyavallade jODupadagaLa baLakeyalli mAtravE
kANisikoLLuva samasyeyEnalla. ondu padavannu yAva sandarbhadalli
baLasalAgide mattu hAge baLasida vyaktiya ASayavEnu embudannu
tiLiyade A padada artha intahadu endu spaShTavAgi hELalu heccinaDe
gaLallU sAdhyavAgadu. udAharaNegAgi, kannaDada halavu padagaLu
(huTTu, taggu, dUru, solu, aLu, taDe ityAdi) nAmapadagaLE
athavA kriyApadagaLE embudannu avugaLa baLakeyinda mAtravE
nirdharisalu sAdhyavide.

(೧ka) avanu dUrida.




(೧kha) avana dUru kELisitu.

(೧ka)dalli dUru embudu kriyApadavAgiyU mattu (೧kha)dalli
nAmapadavAgiyU bandiruvudannu gamanisabahudu. hIgiddarU nAma
pada mattu kriyApadagaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsa kannaDa vyAkaraNadalli
ondu prAmukhyavAda vyatyAsa embudaralli samSayavilla.

padagaLa arthavannu nirdharisuvallU idE rItiyalli baLakeya
sandarbha mattu baLasuvavana ASaya emberaDu viShayagaLu prAmukhya
vAda pAtravannu vahisuttave. bhASheyondaralli baruva padagaLalli heccina
vakkU ondakkinta jAsti arthagaLiddu, ondu baLakeyalli avakke yAva
arthavannu koDabEku embudannu I eraDu viShayagaLa AdhArada
mEle mAtravE nirdharisi hELalu sAdhya,

udAharaNegAgi, kare emba padake 'barahELu' emba arthavU ide,
'hAlannu hinDu' emba arthavU ide. I padavannu obba vyakti
baLasiruvanAdare, avanu adannu yAva arthadalli baLasirabahudu
embudannu A vyaktiya ASaya mattu adannu baLasiruva sandarbha -
iveraDara AdhArada mEle mAtravE nirdharisalu sAdhya. padagaLige I
rIti arthagaLu halaviruvudu aparUpavEnalla embudu ondu artha
kOSada hALegaLannu maguci nODidare sulabhavAgi manadaTTAga
bahudu.


<a id="sec-5-3"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#sec-5-3)

## ೫.೩ jODupadagaLu mattu pratyayaviruva padagaLu

jODupada mattu pratyayaviruva padagaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsavU kelavu
viShayadalli mElina vyatyAsada hAgeyE aspaShTavAgide. Adare idakke
bEreyE ondu kAraNavide. ondu padakke ondu athavA jAsti pratyaya
gaLannu sErisuvudara mUlaka pratyayaviruva pada tayArAguttade mattu
eraDu athavA jAsti padagaLannu oTTige sErisi ondE padavAgi mADu
vudara mUlaka jODupada tayArAguttade embudAgi ivugaLa naDu
viruva vyatyAsavEnO spaShTavAgide, Adare pada mattu pratyayagaLa naDu
viruva vyatyAsa aShTondu spaShTavAdudalla.

udAharaNegAgi, hingAlu emba padadalliruva him embudu
hindu athavA hinde embudara giDDarUpavendu hELidalli adondu
padavenisuttade. idakke badalu adu cAritrikavAgi mAtra hinde embu
dakke sambandhiside endu vAdisidalli adondu pratyayavenisuttade.




idE rItiyalli hejjenu, kengaNNu, ibbadi modalAda padagaLalli
kANisuva hej, ke, ib modalAda amSagaLu padagaLE athavA
pratyayagaLE emba viShayadalli abhiprAyabhEdagaLu kANisalu
sAdhyavide.

pada mattu pratyayagaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsa I rIti aspaShTavAgi
kANisalu mattu vivAdakke eDemADikoDalu mukhya kAraNavEnendare,
cAritrikavAgi heccina pratyayagaLU padagaLinda beLedu bandavugaLu.
modalige svatantravAgidda I padagaLu kramENa giDDavAgi tamma
svAtantryavannu kaLedukoLLuttave mattu pratyayagaLAgi badalAguttave.
sAmAnyavAgi intaha padagaLu bEre sandarbhagaLalli tamma uddarUpa
dalli baruvuvAdare avannu pratyayagaLendu hELade padagaLendu hELu
vudE rUDhi.

udAharaNegAgi, haLegannaDadalli isu embudu ondu svatantra
pada (kriyApada)vAgi baLakeyallittu. adakkidda arthagaLalli 'anumatisu'
embudU ondu embudannu kANalisade, sErisidare modalAda
baLakegaLinda tiLiyabahudu. nEravAgi bEre kriyApadagaLondige sEri
kUDupadagaLAgi bandAgalU (udA: mADisu, baresu, tinnisu,
ityAdi) idakke I arthakke sambandhisidantaha arthavE baruttade.
hAgAgi, haLegannaDada maTTige mADisu, tinnisu modalAda kriyA
rUpagaLalli baruva isu embudannu ondu pratyayavendu hELuva
badalu kriyApadavendu hELuvudE sari.

Adare, hosagannaDadalli isu (illavE su) embudakke svatantra
kriyApadavAgi baLakeyilla. bEre kriyApadagaLondige baresu, karesu,
mADisu modalAda kriyArUpagaLalli mAtravE adu baraballudu.
hAgAgi, hosagannaDada maTTige adondu pratyaya mAtra endu hELa
bEkAguttade.

mEle sUcisidante, cAritrikavAgi ondu padada amSa innondu
padada giDDarUpavAgideyAdarU vartamAna kAladalli averaDaroLage
yAva sambandhavU illa embudAgiyU vAdisalu sAdhyavide. udA
haraNegAgi, mEle modalaneya adhyAyadalli (೧.೧ralli) sUcisidante,
eNNe emba padada eN emba amSa cAritrikavAgi eLLu emba padakke
sambandhiside. Adare kannaDada Adhunika rUpadalli iveraDakke sambandhavannu
kalpisi, eNNe embudu jODupada endu hELalu sAdhyavAgadu.




Adare intaha vivAdaviruva sandarbhagaLallella vayyAkaraNigaLu
yAvudAdarondu nirdhArakke baruva avaSyakateyide. hAgAgi, avaru
antaha ondu nirdhArakke bandAga, pada mattu pratyayagaLa naDuve
kANisuva I aspaShTate mAyavAguttade mattu adarondige jODu
pada mattu pratyayaviruva padagaLa naDuviruva aspaShTateyU mAya
vAguttade.

jODupada mattu pratyayaviruva padagaLa naDuve innondu
rItiya aspaShTateyiruvudannU illi gamanisabahudu. kelavu jODu
padagaLa angagaLAgi eraDu athavA jAsti padagaLu mAtravallade ondu
athavA jAsti pratyayagaLU bandiralu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi,
kasabarike emba padadalli kasa mattu bari(du) emba eraDu padagaLu
mAtravallade, ke emba pratyayavU bandide. hAvADiga emba padadalli
hAvu mattu ADu emba eraDu padagaLu mAtravallade ira emba
pratyayavU sErikonDide.

intaha padagaLannu jODupadagaLendU hELabahudu illavE
pratyayaviruva padagaLendU hELabahudu. Adare sAmAnyavAgi
vyAkaraNa gaLalli I rIti ondakkinta jAsti padagaLiruvavugaLannella
(avugaLondige pratyayagaLu bandirali athavA bAradirali)
jODupadagaLendE kareyu vudu rUDhi.


<a id="sec-5-4"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#sec-5-4)

## ೫.೪ jODupadagaLa guNadharmagaLu

jODupadagaLa eraDu mukhyavAda guNadharmagaLannu nAvu mEleyE
nODiruvevu. padaracaneya niyamagaLige anusAravAgi eraDu athavA
jAsti padagaLu oTTu sEri ondE padavAgive embudu avugaLa ondu
guNadharma; mattu hIge tayArAda padagaLa arthavannu avu hesarisuva
vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa guNadharmada AdhArada mEle mAtravE
nirdharisalu sAdhya embudu avugaLa innondu guNadharma. jODu
padagaLannu vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu hesarisuvudakkAgi baLasabEkA
gideyAda kAraNa, avugaLa arthavannu nEravAgi avugaLa oLaracaneya
AdhArada mEle nirdharisalu sAdhyavAguvudilla.

I eraDu mukhyavAda guNadharmagaLu mAtravallade bEreyU
kelavu guNadharmagaLannu jODupadagaLalli kANalu sAdhyavide. intaha
guNadharmagaLU jODupadagaLannu padagucchagaLinda bErpaDisalu
sahAyakavAgaballuvu. sAmAnyavAgi, padagucchagaLalli baruva padagaLu




bEre bEre svatantra padagaLAgiruttavallade ondE padavAgi oTTu
sEruvudilla. hAgAgi, avugaLa naDuve bEre padagaLannu sErisi hELalu
sAdhyavide. Adare jODupadagaLalli baruva padagaLu oTTu sEri ondE
padavAgiddu tamma svAtantryavannu kaLedukonDive. hAgAgi avugaLa
naDuve bEre padagaLannu nuggisi hELalu sAdhyavAgadu.

udAharaNegAgi, keLagina tuTi emba padagucchadalli keLagina mattu
tuTi emba eraDu svatantravAda padagaLu oTTige bandiveyAdarU bEre
bEre padagaLAgi uLidive. hAgAgi, avugaLa naDuve kempu, oDeda
modalAda bEre padagaLannu irisi, keLagina kempu tuTi, keLagina
oDeda tuTi modalAda avugaLiginta jAsti uddavAda padagucchagaLannu
tayArisi hELalu sAdhyavide. idakke vyatiriktavAgi, keLaduTi emba
jODupadadalli keLa(ge) mattu duTi (tuTi) emba eraDu padagaLu
svatantra padagaLAgi uLidilla mattu I kAraNakkAgi, avugaLa naDuve
bEre padagaLannirisalu sAdhyavAgadu.

heccina padagucchagaLU varNisuva vidhAnada mUlaka vyakti, vastu
modalAduvannu gurutisuvudakkAgi baLakeyAguttave. Adare idakke
apavAdavAgi kannaDadalli kelavu viSiShTavAda padagucchagaLu hesarisuva
vidhAnadallU vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu gurutisuvalli baLakeyAgu
ttave embudannu nAvu mEle mUraneya adhyAyadalli (೩.೩.೭ralli)
nODiruvevu. I rIti hesarisuva vidhAnadalli baLakeyAgiruva pada
gucchagaLa naDuveyU bEre padagaLannu sErisalu sAdhyavAgadu. udA
haraNegAgi, hUvina giDa embudu ondu padagucchavAgideyAdarU
adannu ondu viSiShTavAda giDavannu hesarisuva vidhAnada mUlaka
gurutisuvudakkAgi baLasalAguttade. hAgAgi, adaralli baruva hUvina
mattu giDa emba eraDu padagaLa naDuve bEre padagaLannu (udA:
doDDa embudannu) sErisi hELalu (*hUvina doDDa giDa embudAgi
hELalu) sAdhyavAgadu.

Adare innondu viShayadalli intaha hesarisuva padagucchagaLU
jODupadagaLinda bhinnavAgive. avugaLalli baruva padagaLa arthavannu
bEre bErAgi guNapadagaLa sahAyadinda badalAyisalu sAdhyavide,
Adare jODupadagaLalli bandiruva padagaLa arthavannu I rIti bEre
bErAgi badalAyisalu sAdhyavAgadu. udAharaNegAgi, hUvina giDa
emba padagucchakke bEre padagaLannu sErisuvudara mUlaka adalli




bandiruva eraDu padagaLalli yAvudara arthavannu bEkiddarU badalA
yisalu sAdhyavide.

1. (೨ka) kempu hUvina giDa
2. (೨kha) namma hUvina giDa
3. (೨ga) doDDa hUvina giDa

(೨ka)dalli bandiruva kempu emba pada hUvina giDa emba padagucchada
modalaneya padada arthavannu hecciside. adu 'ondu giDada hU
kempAgide'yendu tiLisuttadallade, 'giDavE kempAgide'yendu tiLisuvu
dilla. Adare (೨kha)dalli namma emba padada mUlaka adE padagucchada
eraDaneya padada arthavannu badalAyisalu sAdhyavAgide. (೨kha)kke
'namma giDa' emba arthavideyallade 'namma hUvu' emba arthavilla.
(೨ga)dalli I eraDu rItiya arthagaLU baralu sAdhyavide. adakke
'doDDa hU biDuva giDa' emba arthavAgalI illavE 'hU biDuva
doDDa giDa' emba arthavAgalI baralu sAdhyaviddu illi arthasandigdhate
yide.

Adare, jODupadagaLa baLakeyalli intaha arthasandigdhategaLige
avakASavilla embudannu gamanisabahudu. idakke kAraNavEnendare,
jODupadadondige baruva padagaLu A padada oTTu arthavEnideyO
adannu mAtra badalAyisaballuvallade adara angagaLAgi baruva
padagaLa arthavannu bEre bErAgi badalAyisalAravu. udAharaNegAgi,
muLLu handi emba jODupadakke cUpAda emba padavannu sErisi A
jODupadada angavAgi bandiruva muLLu emba padada arthavannu
heccisalu sAdhyavAgadu. idE rItiyalli kaNNIru emba jODupadakke
kempu emba guNapadavannu sErisidalli, adu iDI padavu sUcisuva
arthavannu ('kempAgiruva kaNNIru' embudAgi) badalAyisaballudallade
A padada ondu anga sUcisuva arthavannu mAtravE badalAyisa
lAradu. kempu kaNNIru embudakke 'kempAgiruva kaNNina nIru' emba
artha baralAradu.


<a id="sec-5-5"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#sec-5-5)

## ೫.೫ jODupadagaLa oLaracane

pratyayaviruva padagaLa oLaracaneyannu vivarisuvalli mukhyavAgi eraDu
sangatigaLannu pariSIlisidare sAkAgittu. avugaLalli yAva pratyayagaLannu




baLasalAgide embudannU mattu I pratyayagaLannu yAva vargakke
sErida padagaLondige (endare nAmapada, kriyApada illavE guNapada
gaLondige) baLasalAgide embudannU pariSIlisidare sAkAgittu. kelavu
pratyayaviruva padagaLalli hIge pada mattu pratyayagaLannu oTTige sErisu
vAga avugaLalli kelavu badalAvaNegaLu naDeyuvuvAda kAraNa, intaha
badalAvaNegaLannU 'sErikeya niyama'gaLu (illavE sandhiniyamagaLu)
emba hesarinalli varNisuva avaSyakateyittu.

jODupadagaLa oLaracaneyannu vivarisuvAga I rIti avugaLa
racaneyalli baLakeyAguva padagaLu, avugaLa padavarga mattu avugaLa
racaneya hindiruva sErikeya niyamagaLu emba I mUru viShaya
gaLannu mAtravallade, A padagaLa naDuviruva sambandhavEnu embudannU
vivarisi hELuva krama rUDhiyallide. padagaLeraDannu I rIti
sambandhisalu ondu vAkya illavE vAkyAmSavannu baLasabEkAgiddu,
idannu samskxta vyAkaraNagaLalli mattu avugaLannanusarisuva kannaDa
vyAkaraNagaLalli 'vigraha vAkya' endu kareyalAgide.

kannaDadalli ivu heccinaDegaLallU vAkyarUpadallirade ondu pada
gucchada rUpadalliruttave. hAgAgi ivannu 'vAkya' endu kareyuvudu
kannaDada maTTigantU aShTondu txptikaravAgilla. jODupadagaLa oLa
racaneyannu sUkShmavAgi vivarisi hELuvudakkAgi ivu baLakeyAguttive
yAda kAraNa I viShayavannu sUcisuva jODupadagaLa 'oLanuDi'
emba hesarannu illi baLasalAgide.

udAharaNegAgi, mincuhuLa emba jODupadadalli mincu
mattu huLa emba eraDu padagaLu oTTu sErive. I padagaLa
naDuviruva sambandhavannu mincuva huLa emba padagucchada vivarisa
bahudu. I huLa mincuttade emba vAkya I sambandhavannu innaShTu
spaShTavAgi tOrisikoDuttade. idE rItiyalli talegUdalu emba
jODupadada angagaLAgi bandiruva tale mattu kUdalu emberaDu
padagaLa naDuviruva sambandhavannu taleya kUdalu illavE taleyalli
beLeyuva kUdalu emba padaguccha tOrisikoDuttade. intaha
padagucchagaLannu (illavE heccu vivaravAgi oLaracaneyannu tiLisuva
vAkyagaLannu) A jODupadagaLa oLanuDigaLendu hELabahudu.

jODupadagaLa oLaracaneyantahadu embudannu tiLiyalu I rIti
avugaLalli bandiruva padagaLa naDuviruva sambandhavannU tiLiyuvudu
yAke avaSya embudannu spaShTapaDisalu bEre kelavu udAharaNegaLannu




gamanisabahudu. naDuberaLu mattu naDuhagalu emba eraDu jODu
padagaLallU mElininda mEle nODuvAga oLaracane ondE rItiya
dendu anisuttade. eraDarallU naDu emba guNapadadondige nAma
padavondannu (beraLu illavE hagalu embudannu) sErisi hELiruvu
dannu kANabahudu.

Adare I eraDu padagaLa naDuviruva sambandha mAtra mEle
koTTiruva jODupadagaLalli bEre bErAgide. naDuberaLu embudu
kayyalli aydu beraLugaLa naDuvinalliruva beraLannu gurutisuvudAda
kAraNa, adaralli naDu emba guNapada beraLu emba padada arthavannu
heccisuvudakkAgi bandideyendu hELalu sAdhyavide. hAgAgi avugaLa
naDuviruva sambandhavannu naDuvina beraLu emba padaguccha sariyAgi
sUcisaballudu. Adare naDuhagalu emba jODupada 'naDuvinalliruva
hagala'nnu sUcisuvudilla, idakke badalu adu 'hagalina naDubhAgavannu'
sUcisuttade. hAgAgi, I jODupadadalli bandiruva naDu mattu
hagalu emba padagaLa naDuviruva sambandhavannu naDuvina hagalu emba
padagucchada mUlaka sUcisalu sAdhyavAgadu. idakke badalAgi, hagalina
naDubhAga emba bErondu rItiya padagucchavannu illi baLasabEkAgu
ttade.

idE rItiyalli keLaduTi embudakke keLagina tuTi (illavE
mukhadalli keLage iruva tuTi) emba oLanuDiyannu (vigrahavAkyavannu)
koDalu sAdhyavide; Adare tudigAlu embudakke adE rItiyalli
tudiya kAlu (illavE tudiyalliruva kAlu) embudAgi
oLanuDinnu koTTalli adu sariyAgalAradu. I eraDaneya jODu
padakke kAlina tudi illavE kAlina tudiyalliruva bhAga embudAgi
oLanuDiyannu hELabEkAguttade. I eraDu jODupadagaLallU
nAmapadavondakke guNapadavondannu sErisi hELalAgideyAdarU
avugaLa naDuviruva sambandha ondE alla embudannu I eraDu bhinna
bhinnavAda oLanuDigaLu tiLisuttave.

jODupadagaLa angagaLAgi baruva padagaLannu I rIti oLanuDigaLa
mUlaka sambandhisuvalli ondu mukhyavAda samasyeyide embudannilli
gamanisuvudu avaSya. nAvu mUraneya adhyAyadalli (೩.೩.೧ralli)
nODiruvante, jODupadagaLa tayArike mattu baLakegaLa naDuve
asAngatyaviralu sAdhyavide. avannu tayArisuva samayadalli avu
hesarisabEkAgiruva vyakti illavE vastuvinalli kaNNige eddu kANisu




vantaha yAvudAdarU ondu guNadharmavannu AdhAravAgirisikonDu
avannu racisirabEku. Adare avugaLa baLakeyAguttiruva samayadalli I
guNadharma A vyakti illavE vastuvinalli hAgeyE uLiyabEkendEnU
illa.

udAharaNegAgi, hosamane emba pada bahaLa haLeyadAgiruva
ondu maneyannu hesarisuttiralu sAdhyavide. A manege hosamane
embudAgi hesaru koDuva samayadalli adu hattiradallidda uLida
ellA manegaLindalU hosatAgiddirabEku; anantara A hesaru baLake
yAguttiruva samayadalli adu kramENa haLeyadAguttA bandarU,
mattu hattiravE bEre manegaLu hosadAgi mEleddiveyAdarU,
hosamane emba adara hesarannu badalisi haLemane endu hELalu
yArU prayatnisuvudilla. ondu hesarina baLakege (endare adara
arthakke) adara oLaracaneyinda dorakuva artha AdhAravAguvudilla
vembudE idakke kAraNa.

jODupadagaLa tayArike mattu A tayArikeyalli baLakeyAguva
guNadharma iveraDU A padagaLa caritrege sambandhisida viShayagaLendu
hELabahudu. avugaLa baLake mattu baLakege sambandhisida guNadharma
(endare avugaLa Igina artha) iveraDU Igina kAlakke sambandhisida
viShayagaLu. jODupadavondara oLaracaneyannu vivarisuvAga adaralli
baruva padagaLannu sambandhisuvantaha oLanuDigaLannu iveraDu viShaya
gaLalli yAvudara AdhArada mEle hELabEku (cAritrika AdhArada
mElO athavA Igina kAlakke sambandhisida viShayagaLa AdhArada
mElO) embudE illi taledOruva samasye. sAmAnyavAgi jODu
padagaLa tayArikege sambandhisidantaha cAritrika amSagaLa AdhArada
mElEnE oLanuDigaLannu hELuvudu rUDhiyAdarU, adu A padagaLa
Igina baLakeyentahadu (endare adara arthaventahadu) embudannu
sUcisuvantiddare oLLeyadu endU anisadiruvudilla.

kelavomme iveraDannU hondisikoLLalu sAdhyavAgadirabahudu.
udAharaNegAgi, hosamane emba jODupada bahaLa haLeyadAgiruva
ondu maneyannu hesarisuvudAdarU adara oLanuDiyannu hosa
dAda mane endE koDabEkAguttade. A maneyalli Iga kANisuva
yAva guNadharmavU I oLanuDige AdhAravAgalAradu. idE rIti
yalli ugibanDi emba jODupada ivattu ugiya badalu DIsel
illavE vidyucchaktiyannu baLasi ODuva sAdhanavannu hesarisuvudE jAsti




yAgideyAdarU A padada oLanuDiyannu uriya sahAyadinda
calisuva banDi endE koDabEkAguttade. oLanuDigaLu jODupadagaLa
angagaLAgi bandiruva padagaLannu sambandhisuvantirabEkembudE I rIti
jODupadagaLa oLanuDigaLigU mattu avugaLa arthakkU naDuve
kANisuva asAngatyavannu toDedu hAkalu sAdhyavilladante mADide.

bahuSaH intaha sandarbhagaLalli jODupadagaLige avugaLa 'caritre
yannu sUcisuva oLanuDi' mattu 'Igina arthavannu sUcisuva oLa
nuDi' embudAgi eraDu rItiya oLanuDigaLannu koDalu sAdhya
vAdItu. udAharaNegAgi hosamane emba padakke adara caritreyannu
sUcisuva hosadAda mane emba oLanuDiyannU mattu adara
ivattina arthavannu sUcisuva haLeyadAgiruva mane emba oLanuDi
yannU hELalu sAdhyavAdItu. Adare intaha oLanuDigaLalli
eraDaneyadu jODupadada 'oLaracane'yannu vivarisuttade endu
hELuvudu mAtra svalpa kaShTa. yAkendare, hosamane emba jODu
padada oLaracaneyalli haLeyadAgiruva emba amSavannAgali, illavE
ugibanDi emba jODupadada oLaracaneyalli DIsel athavA
vidyucchaktiyannu baLasuva emba amSavannAgali kANisuvudu kaShTa.

ondu jODupadada caritreyannu sUcisaballantaha oLanuDiyannu
kanDuhiDiyuvudarallU halakelavu samasyegaLELaballuvu. yAkendare,
sAmAnyavAgi nAvu ondu jODupadada ivattina baLakeya AdhArada
mEle mattu adara oLaracaneya AdhArada mEle, adara tayArikeyalli
entaha guNadharma baLakeyAgiddirabEku endu UhisabEkAguttade.
hIge UhisikoLLuvAga nAvu tappibILalu sAdhyavide mattu kelavomme
ondakkinta jAsti oLanuDigaLannu koDalu sAdhyaviddu avugaLalli
yAvudu jODupadada tayArikeyalli baLakeyAgidda nijavAda
cAritrika ghaTaneyannu sUcisuttade embudannu nirdharisalu sAdhyavAga
dirabahudu.

udAharaNegAgi, ugibanDi emba jODupadakke ugiya sahAya
dinda calisuva banDi endAgali, illavE ugiyannu uguLuttA
calisuva banDi endAgali cAritrika oLanuDiyannu koDalu sAdhyavide.
Adare ivugaLalli yAvudu sari embudannu nirdharisalu ugibanDi
emba jODupadavannu tayArisidAga I eraDu oLanuDigaLu
sUcisuva guNadharmagaLalli yAvudannu gamanadallirisikoLLalAgittu
emba cAritrika amSa mAtravE AdhAravAgaballudu. Adare intaha




cAritrika amSagaLannu kanDuhiDiyuvudu kaShTasAdhyavAda kAraNa, I rIti
ondakkinta jAsti oLanuDigaLannu koDalu sAdhyaviruva sandarbhagaLalli
yAvudu sari mattu yAvudu tappu endu nirdharisalu sAdhyavAgadu.

## ೫. jODupadagaLa vibhajane

kannaDada jODupadagaLannu avugaLalli kANisuva vyatyAsagaLa AdhArada
mEle bEre bEre rItiyalli vingaDisi hELalu sAdhyavide. sAmAnyavAgi
avugaLa oLaracaneyalli kANisuva vyatyAsagaLannE intaha vibhajanege
AdhAravAgi tegedukoLLuvudu rUDhi. jODupadagaLa angagaLAgi
baruva padagaLa sankhye mattu padavarga, I padagaLa naDuviruva
sambandha, mattu jODupadagaLa kEndrabindu avugaLa oLageyE
ideyE athavA horagideyE, oLagideyAdare yAva padada mElide
(modalinadara mEleyE athavA koneyadara mEleyE) embantaha
viShayagaLa AdhArada mEle kannaDada jODupadagaLannu bEre bEre
gumpugaLAgi vingaDisi hELalu sAdhyavide.

illi gamanisabEkAgiruva ondu mukhya amSavEnendare, jODu
padagaLa I vibhajanegaLella avugaLa oLaracaneya mEle mattu antaha
racaneyalli baLakeyAguva padagaLa svabhAvada mEle avalambisideyAda
kAraNa, ivu jODupadagaLa caritrege sambandhisida vibhajanegaLallade
avugaLa Igina baLakege sambandhisiduvalla. baLakege sambandhisidante
kannaDada nAmapadagaLannu hEge vibhajisabahudembudannu nAvu mEleyE
(೩.೫ralli) nODiruvevu. jODupadagaLannU idE vidhAnada mUlaka
ankitanAma, rUDhanAma ityAdiyAgi vingaDisalu sAdhyavide. Adare
idu jODupadagaLige mAtra anvayisuva vibhajaneyAgalAradu, mattu
jODupadagaLa viSiShTa guNagaLa mEle avalambisuva vibhajaneyU Aga
lAradu.

kannaDadalli 'kriyAsamAsa' embondu samAsavideyendu kESirAja
ninda Arambhisi halavAru vayyAkaraNigaLu hELuttiddAre. hAgAgi,
kannaDada jODupadagaLannu nAmapada mattu kriyApada embudAgi
eraDu vidhadavugaLendu vingaDisalu sAdhya emba abhiprAya kelavaradira
bahudu. Adare I 'kriyAsamAsa'dinda tayArAguva vAkyAmSagaLella
padagucchagaLallade jODupadagaLalla embudannu munde (೫.೮.೮ralli)
nODaliruvevu. hAgAgi 'kriyAsamAsa'vembudu kannaDadalli samAsa
valla emba nirdhArakke barabEkAguttade. jODupadagaLigU mattu




padagucchagaLigU naDuviruva vyatyAsavannu nAmapadagaLalli mAtra
kANaballevallade kriyApada illavE guNapadagaLalli kANalArevembudE
I rIti jODupadagaLu nAmapadagaLAgi mAtra baraballuvembudakke
mukhya kAraNa.

kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLalli kANisuva ('samAsa'gaLemba hesarina) jODu
padagaLa vibhajanege mEle sUcisida vyatyAsagaLalli halavannu oTTAgi
baLasalAguttade. samskxta vyAkaraNagaLalli baLakeyalliruva vibhajaneyannu
hAgeyE kannaDakke aLavaDisalAgideyAda kAraNa, kannaDada maTTige idu
svalpavU txptikaravAgilla embudannu nAvu mundina ondu vibhAgadalli
(೫.೮ralli) nODaliruvevu.


<a id="sec-5-6-1"></a>

## ೫.೬.೧ sankhyeyannu baLasuva vibhajane

jODupadagaLannu avugaLa angagaLAgi baruva padagaLa sankhyeya
AdhArada mEle vingaDisi hELalu sAdhyavide. Adare kannaDadalli baruva
jODupadagaLalli heccinavU eraDu padagaLa sErikeyinda mAtravE
tayArAdavugaLAda kAraNa intaha vibhajane kannaDada maTTige jAsti
upayuktavalla. eraDakkinta jAsti padagaLinda tayArAda jODupada
gaLu kannaDadalli bahaLa aparUpa.

jODupadagaLa oLaracaneyalli padagaLu mAtravallade pratyayagaLU
baralu sAdhyaviddu, intaha jODupadagaLannu uLida jODupadagaLinda
bErpaDisi hELalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi, dArihOka embuda
ralli dAri mattu hOgu emberaDu padagaLu mAtravallade a emba
pratyayavU kANisuttade. (I pratyaya sEridAga hOgu embudara
koneya ukAra bidduhOguttade mattu gakAra kakAravAguttade).

idE rItiyalli hAvADiga embudaralli hAvu mattu ADu
emba padagaLu mAtravallade iga emba pratyayavU kANisuttade.
kannaDadalli *hOka mattu *ADiga embavugaLu svatantra padagaLAgi
baLakeyallillavAda kAraNa I rIti mElina jODupadagaLalli eraDu
padagaLondige ondu pratyayavU sErikonDideyendu hELuva avaSya
kateyunTAguttade. Adare bEre viShayagaLalli ivu eraDu padagaLinda
tayArAda itara jODupadagaLa hAgeyE (udA: bayalATa, tale
tiruka, ityAdi) kANisuvuvAda kAraNa, ivu tayArAguva samayadalli
*hOka, *ADiga modalAdavugaLu svatantra padagaLAgidduvendu kalpisi
koLLalU sAdhyavide.





<a id="sec-5-6-2"></a>

## ೫.೬.೨ padavargagaLannu baLasuva vibhajane

jODupadagaLannu tayArisalu baLasiruva padagaLu yAva padavargakke
sErive emba viShayada AdhArada mEle avannu mUru mukhya vibhAga
gaLalli vingaDisalu sAdhyavide. kannaDada heccina jODupadagaLallU
eraDaneya anga nAmapadavAgiruttade. modalaneyadu mAtra nAma
padavirabahudu, kriyApadavirabahudu illavE guNapadavirabahudu. I
kAraNakkAgi, kannaDada heccina jODupadagaLannU avugaLa modalaneya
angavAgi baruva padagaLa vargavannAdharisi nAmapadaviruvavu, kriyA
padaviruvavu mattu guNapadaviruvavu embudAgi mUru mukhya
vibhAgagaLalli vingaDisi hELabahudu.

*modalaneya angavAgi nAmapada bandiruva jODupadagaLu*

jODupadagaLalli eraDaneya angavAgi baruva pada nAmapada
vAgiruva badalu kriyApadavAgiralU sAdhyavideyembudannu (udA:
kaypiDi, bAnuli), munde (೫.೬.೩ralli) nODaliruvevu. adakke
modalu kannaDadalli mukhyavAgi baruva mEle hELida mUru rItiya
jODupadagaLa svarUpaventahadembudannu I keLage svalpa vivaravAgi
pariSIlisalAgide.




## (ka) modalaneya anga nAmapadavAgiruva jODupadagaLu

eraDu nAmapadagaLannu oTTu sErisuvudara mUlaka tayArAgiruva
jODupadagaLu kannaDadalli halavive. ivugaLalli heccinavU a emba
sambandhaka pratyayada mUlaka eraDu nAmapadagaLannu oTTu sErisuvu
dara mUlaka tayArAdavugaLu. udA:

<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>ಒಳನುಡಿ</th>
<th>ಜೋಡುಪದ</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>ಬಯಲಿನ ಆಟ</td>
<td>ಬಯಲಾಟ</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ಬೆಂಕಿಯ ಪೆಟ್ಟಿಗೆ</td>
<td>ಬೆಂಕಿಪೆಟ್ಟಿಗೆ</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ನೆಲದ ಕಡಲೆ</td>
<td>ನೆಲಿಕಡಲೆ</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ಕಾಲಿನ ಮಣೆ</td>
<td>ಕಾಲ್ಮಣಿ</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ಕೈಯ ಮಗ್ಗ</td>
<td>ಕೈಮಗ್ಗ</td>
</tr>
</tbody>

I rIti sambandhaka pratyayada mUlaka tayArAgiruva jODupada
gaLa naDuveyU halakelavu vyatyAsagaLive. I vyatyAsagaLannu tOrisi
koDalu ivakke sambandhaka pratyayada mUlaka oLanuDigaLannu hELuva
badalu bEre bEre vibhakti pratyayagaLannu baLasi oLanuDigaLannu hELa
bEkAguttade, mattu idakkAgi I oLanuDigaLalli jODupadagaLalli
kANisadiruvantaha bEre bEre kriyApadagaLannU baLasikoLLabEkAguttade.
sAmAnyavAgi eraDu nAmapadagaLa naDuvina sambandhavannu jAsti
vivaragaLannu koDade cuTukAgi sUcisalu sambandhaka pratyayavannu
baLasuttEve. I pratyaya eraDu nAmapadagaLannu nEravAgi sambandhisu
ttade. vibhakti pratyayagaLu I rIti eraDu nAmapadagaLannu nEravAgi
sambandhisuvudilla. idakke badalu avu yAvudAdarondu kriyApadavu
sUcisuva ghaTaneyalli nAmapadagaLu hesarisuva vyakti, vastu modalA
davugaLu yAva rItiyalli niratavAgive embudannu tiLisuvudara
mUlaka antaha nAmapadagaLannu sambandhisuttave.

udAharaNegAgi, kaNNina nIru embudaralli kaNNu emba pada
dondige bandiruva sambandhaka pratyaya kaNNigU mattu nIrigU
naDuviruva sambandhavannu nEravAgi sUcisuttade. idakke badalu,
kaNNinalli baruva nIru embudaralli adE kaNNu emba padadondige
bandiruva alli emba vibhakti pratyaya baru emba kriyApadavu
sUcisuva ghaTaneyalli kaNNu mattu nIru embavugaLu yAva




rItiyalli niratavAgive (kaNNu AkaravAgi mattu nIru antaha Akaradalli
kANisuva vastuvAgi) embudannu tiLisuvudara mUlaka sambandhisuttade.

idE rItiyalli jEnina huLa embudaralli kANisuva sambandhaka
pratyaya jEnu mattu huLa emba eraDu nAmapadagaLannu nEravAgi
sambandhisuvudAdare, jEnannu sangrahisuva huLa embudaralli baruva
annu emba vibhakti pratyaya sangrahisu emba ghaTaneyalli jEnu
mattu huLa emba padagaLu yAva rItiyalli sangrahisu emba
kriyApadadondige sambandhisive embudannu tiLisuvudara mUlaka A
eraDu nAmapadagaLa naDuviruva sambandhavannu suttu baLasi hELuttave.

I rIti sambandhaka pratyayada badalu bEre bEre vibhakti pratyaya
gaLannu (kriyApadagaLondige) baLasuvudara mUlaka eraDu nAmapada
gaLiruva jODupadagaLalli heccina vayvidhyateyannu tOrisalu sAdhyavide
mattu I vayvidhyateya AdhArada mEle avannu bEre bEre gumpugaLalli
vingaDisalu sAdhyavide. intaha oLanuDigaLalli yAva vibhakti pratyaya
bandide embudu I vibhajanege ondu AdhAravAgaballudu.

jODupada sambandhaka pratyaya vibhakti pratyayagaLu
jEnuhuLa jEnina huLa jEnannu sangrahisuva huLa
aDakattari aDakeya kattari aDakeyannu kattarisuva kattari
benkipeTTige benkiya peTTige benkiyannu mADalu baLasuva
peTTige
kaNNusanne kaNNina sanne kaNNininda mADida sanne
nUlENi nUlina ENi nUlininda mADida ENi
kaykoDali kayya koDali kayyinda kaDiyalu baLasuva
koDali
mUrudAra mUgina dAra (ettina) mUrige kaTTida dAra
tappu kANike tappina kANike tappige koDuva kANike
kaynIru kayya nIru (maduveyalli) kayge ereyuva
nIru
kaNNIru kaNNina nIru kaNNinalli baruva nIru
talegUdalu taleya kUdalu taleyalli beLeyuva kUdalu
kALLiccu kADina kiccu kADinalli uriyuva kiccu (benki)




mEle modalaneya kAlannalli koTTiruva jODupadagaLigella a
emba sambandhaka pratyayavannu baLasi ondE rItiya oLanuDigaLannu
koDalu sAdhyavideyembudannu eraDaneya kAlannindalU mattu annu,
inda, ge mattu alli emba bEre bEre vibhakti pratyayagaLallondannu
baLasi avakkEnE bEre bEre rItiya oLanuDigaLannu koDalu sAdhyavide
yembudannu mUraneya kAlannindalU tiLiyabahudu.

I rIti bEre bEre vibhakti pratyayagaLalli yAvudara mUlaka I
jODupadagaLa angagaLAgi baruva nAmapadagaLannu sambandhisabahudu
emba viShayada AdhArada mEle avannu vingaDisuva badalu, hAge
sambandhisuvudakkAgi baLasuva kriyApadagaLu yAvuvu emba viShayada
AdhArada mElU ivannu vingaDisalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi, keLage
koTTiruva jODupadagaLigella mADu emba kriyApadavannu baLasi
oLanuDiyannu tayArisalu sAdhyavide.
