I pratyayavannu sErisidAga guNapadadalli aniyamitavAgi bEre
bEre rItiya badalAvaNegaLu naDeyuttave. udAharaNegAgi, biLi, bisi
mattu midu embavugaLa modalaneya akSharadalliruva ikAra ekAra
vAguttade. (nijakkU illi naDediruva cAritrika badalAvaNe idakke
viruddhavAdudu: pUrvada haLegannaDadalli I svara ellA kaDegaLallU
ekAravAgittu; Adare anantara biLi, bisi modalAdavugaLa eraDaneya




akSharadalli ikAra bandideyAda kAraNa adu ikAravAgittu, mattu
beccage, beLLage modalAda padagaLa eraDaneya akSharadalli ikArada
badalu akAravideyAda kAraNa, A ekAra badalAgade hAgeyE uLi
dittu.)

age emba pratyayavannoLagonDiruva bEreyU kelavu guNapada
gaLu kannaDadalliveyAdarU avakke nEravAgi bEre guNapadagaLondige
sambandhavannu sAdhisalu sAdhyavAguvudilla. udAharaNegAgi teppage
emba padavannu teravu emba nAmapadadondige hOlisidAga adaralli
I pratyayavideyendu anisuttade. I age emba pratyaya nAmapada
gaLondige baruva ge emba vibhakti pratyayakke sambandhiside embudannu
kone emba nAmapadadinda tayArAgiruva konege emba pada
sUcisu ttade.

nijakkU vibhakti pratyayagaLondige baruva nAmapadagaLigU mattu
kriyApadagaLondige baruva guNapadagaLigU naDuve hattirada sambandha
vide. vibhakti pratyayagaLu nAmapadagaLannu kriyApadagaLondige sambandhi
suttave mattu I kAraNakkAgi, avu ondu rItiyalli guNapadagaLa hAge
kriyApadagaLa viSEShaNagaLAgiveyendU hELalu sAdhyavide.


<a id="sec-7-5"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#sec-7-5)

## ೭.೫ sArAmSa

guNapadagaLa racaneyallU pratyayagaLa baLake jAstiyilla. nAmapada
gaLondige baraballa guNapadagaLinda kriyApadagaLondige baraballa guNa
padagaLannu tayArisuvudakkAgi mAtra, halavu padagaLalli kANisikoLLuva
age emba pratyaya baLakeyAguttade. idannu biTTare pratyayagaLa baLake
heccAgi kANisikoLLuvudu SabdagaLannu illavE anubhavagaLannu aNakisu
vantaha padagaLa baLakeyalli mAtra.




<a id="adhyAya-8"></a>

[English →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-en#chapter-8--internal-structure-of-loanwords) | [ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#adhyAya-8)

## adhyAya enTu
eravalu padagaLa oLaracane


<a id="sec-8-1"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#sec-8-1)

## ೮.೧ eraDaneya svarUpa

kannaDadalli samskxta, ingliSh, hindi, parSiyan modalAda bEre
bEre bhAShegaLinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLu halavive. ivugaLa
oLaracane hindina adhyAyagaLalli vivarisida kannaDa padagaLa oLaracaneginta
bhinna vAgiruvudAda kAraNa avannu pratyEkavAgi pariSIlisuva
avaSyakateyide. antaha pariSIlaneyannu I adhyAyadalli mADalAgide.
Adare kannaDadavE Ada padagaLu mattu bEre bhAShegaLinda
eravalAgi banda padagaLu embudAgi kannaDadalli baLakeyalliruva pada
gaLannu eraDu bEre bEre vargagaLalli vibhajisi hELuvudu mAtra
aShTondu sulabhada kelasavEnalla. yAkendare anAdi kAladindalU
intaha padagaLa eravalu namma bhASheyalli naDeyuttiddu, I
prakriyeya mUlaka adaralli sErikonDiruva padagaLalli bahaLa ittIcege
bandavugaLu mAtra tammatanavannu uLisikonDu bEre rItiya padagaLa
hAge kANisuttave. uLiduvella bEre bEre badalAvaNegaLa mUlaka
kannaDadavE AgibiTTive.


<a id="sec-8-1-1"></a>

## ೮.೧.೧ bhAShegaLoLage eraDalinalli vayvidhya

ellA bhAShegaLigU ondalla ondu vidhadalli bEre bhAShegaLondige
samparkaviddE iruttadeyAda kAraNa, ellA bhAShegaLallU eravalAgi
banda padagaLu iddE iruttave. kelavu bhAShegaLalli intaha padagaLu
jAsti iruttave, mattu bEre kelavu bhAShegaLalli kaDime iruttave



embudE I viShayadalli bEre bEre bhAShegaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsa. I
vyatyAsakke halavu kAraNagaLive.

padagaLannu eravalu koDuva bhAShegU mattu eravalu paDeyuva
bhAShegU naDuve bahaLa hattirada samparkavideyAdare, mattu eravalu
koDuva bhAShe heccu pratiShTheyadAdare, heccu heccu padagaLu adarinda
eralAgi bandu eravalu paDeyuva bhASheyalli sErikoLLalu sAdhyavide.
kannaDada maTTige samskxta bahaLa pratiShTheya bhASheyAgittAda kAraNa
adarinda doDDa sankhyeyalli padagaLu kannaDakke eravalAgi bandive.
ivattu ingliSh bhAShe antahadE pratiShTheya sthAnadallideyAda kAraNa
adarindalU padagaLu heccina sankhyeyalli eravalAgi baruttive.

idallade, ondu bhASheyannADuva janara manasthitiyantahadu,
avaru sulabhavAgi padagaLa eravalige marehoguvavarE athavA hosa
hosa padagaLannu baLasabEkAguva sandarbha bandAgalella tammavE Ada
padagaLannu sxShTisikoLLuvavarE embudu I vyatyAsakke innondu
AdhAravAguttade. tamma bhASheya kuritAgi jAsti abhimAnavannu
hondiruva mandi eravaligintalU hosa padagaLa tayArikegEnE kay
hAkuvudu jAsti.

bhASheyallillada hosa padagaLa avaSyakate bEre bEre kAraNagaLigAgi
kANisikoLLuttade. bErondu bhASheyannADuva janaralli baLakeyalliruva
vastugaLu nammalli baLakege bandAga, antaha vastugaLannu hesarisuvu
dakkAgi namage hosa padagaLa avaSyakate kanDubaruttade. intaha
sandarbhagaLalli A vastugaLondige avugaLa hesarugaLannU nAvu Amadu
mADikoLLabahudu, illavE nammavE Ada hesarugaLannu tayArisi
avakke koDabahudu.

udAharaNegAgi, ingliSh bhASheyannADuva samAjadinda nAvu
rEDiyO, Ti.vi., bassu, kAru, pennu, raylu, kampyUTar modalAda
halavAru vastugaLannu baLakege paDediddu, avugaLondige A vastugaLa
hesarugaLannU eravalAgi paDedukonDiddEve. intaha vastugaLalli kela
vakke (udA: ugibanDi) nammavE Ada hesarugaLannu koTTiruvevAdarU
bEre kelavakke avugaLa hesarugaLannE alpa svalpa badalAvaNegaLondige
uLisikonDiddEve.

I rIti hosa hosa rItiya vastugaLannu baLakege paDedukoLLu
vudu mAtravalla, hosa hosa viShayagaLannU nAvu bEre bhAShegaLa
nnADuva janarinda tiLidukoLLuvavAddarinda antaha viShayagaLannu




hesarisuva padagaLU namma bhAShege eravalAgi baruttave. I rItiyalli
eravAlAgi bandiruva nUrAru padagaLannu SAstrIya granthagaLalli kANa
bahudu. namma dinanityada baLakeyalliruva bhASheyallU intaha hala
vAru padagaLu bEre bhAShegaLinda eravalAgi bandu sErikonDiruttave.

## A.೧.೨ tattva mattu tadbhava padagaLu

I rIti eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLalli samskxta bhASheyinda bandavu
gaLannu mAtra avugaLa svarUpavannAdharisi tadbhava mattu tadbhava
embudAgi vingaDisi hELuva krama kannaDada vyAkaraNagaLalli mattu
arthakOSagaLalli baLakeyallide. samskxtadalli iruva hAgeyE baLake
yAguva padagaLu (endare samskxtada padagaLige samAnavAda padagaLu)
tadbhavagaLu mattu antaha padagaLalli bEre bEre rItiya badalAvaNe
gaLAdudarindAgi avugaLiginta bhinnavAgiruva padagaLu tadbhavagaLu
(endare samskxtadinda janisida padagaLu) embudAgi I vibhajaneyannu
varNisabahudu. Adare, sAmAnyavAgi padagaLa koneya bhAgadalli
mAtravE badalAvaNeyAgideyAdare, antaha padagaLannu tadbhavagaLendu
hELade tadbhavagaLendu hELuvudE rUDhi (SrIkanThayya ೧೯೫೨:೧೯೬
nODi).

udAharaNegAgi, yAva badalAvaNeyannU tOrisadiruva satya,
dharma, adhikAri, kapi modalAdavugaLannu mattu koneyalli mAtravE
badalAvaNeyannu tOrisuva SAle (SAlA), janani (jananI),
manassu (manas) modalAdavugaLannu tatsama padagaLendU mattu
itara bhAgagaLalli badalAvaNegaLannu tOrisuva Ase (ASA), nidde
(nidrA), huNNime (pUrNimA), batti (varti) modalAda padagaLannu
tadbhava padagaLendU kareyuva krama rUDhiyallide.

intaha padagaLa vibhajane inDO-Aryan emba bhAShAkuTumbakke
sEriruva prAkxta, pAli, hindi, marAThi, gujarAti modalAda bhAShegaLa
vyAkaraNa mattu arthakOSagaLa maTTige bahaLa upayuktavAdudendu
hELalu sAdhyavide. nijakkU I bhAShegaLalli tatsama mattu tadbhava emba
eraDu rItiya padagaLu mAtra ive. ivugaLalli tadbhava padagaLella
cAritrikavAgi samskxtakkU mattu avakkU oTTige mUla bhASheyA
giruva inDO-Aryan‌ninda beLedubandavugaLu. samskxtada padagaLi
ginta bhinnavAgilladiruva tatsama padagaLu mAtra nEravAgi samskxtadinda
eravalAgi bandavugaLu embudAgi parigaNisalu sAdhyavide.




Adare kannaDa bhAShe idakkinta tIra bhinnavAgiruva drAviDa bhAShA
kuTumbakke sEriruva kAraNa, adaralli tatsama mattu tadbhava padagaLu
mAtravallade mUla bhASheyinda beLedu bandiruva drAviDa padagaLU
halavive. nijakkU kannaDadalli kANisuva tatsama mattu tadbhava
padagaLeraDU samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda padagaLE. avugaLa
naDuviruva vyatyAsavEnendare, tatsama padagaLalli kaDime badalAvaNegaLu
naDedive mattu tadbhava padagaLalli jAsti badalAvaNegaLu naDedive.
hAgAgi, kannaDada vyAkaraNa illavE arthakOSada maTTige tatsama-
tadbhavavemba eravalu padagaLa vibhajaneyinda viSiShTavAda prayOjana
vEnU illa. kannaDada maTTige samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda padagaLa
nnella ondE vibhAgadalli irisi pariSIlisidare sAkAguttade.

## A.೧.೩ badalAvaNegaLige kAraNagaLu

eravalAgi banda padagaLu bEre bEre kAraNagaLigAgi badalAvaNegaLige
oLagAguttave. avannu eravalAgi koTTa bhAShegU mattu eravalAgi
paDedukonDa bhAShegU naDuve varNagaLa sankhyeya maTTige mattu
varNagaLu padagaLalli baruva kramada maTTige vyatyAsagaLiveyAdare,
padagaLannu eravalAgi paDeyuva bhAShe tanna varNavyavasthege hondi
koLLuvante avugaLalli badalAvaNegaLannu mADikoLLuttade. udAharaNe
gAgi kannaDadalli mahAprANAkSharagaLu mUlataH iralillavAdudarinda,
samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda halavAru padagaLalli mahAprANakSharagaLu
alpaprANAkSharagaLAgi badalAgive. udA: bIdi (vIthi), sante
(samsthA), dAre (dhArA), bandi (bandhi), ityAdi.

innondu bhASheyinda jAsti padagaLannu eravalu paDediruva bhAShe
avugaLondige kelavu hosa varNagaLannU paDedukonDiralu sAdhyavide,
mattu anantara A bhASheyinda eravalAgi baruva padagaLalli antaha
varNagaLu badalAgade uLiyalu sAdhyavide. kannaDada kelavu prabhEda
gaLalli (udA: barahada kannaDa) I rIti heccu heccu mahA
prANAkSharagaLiruva padagaLu eravalAgi bandudarindAgi antaha akShara
gaLu A prabhEdada varNagaLAgibiTTive. tatsama mattu tadbhavagaLemba
eraDu rItiya eravalAda padagaLu kannaDadalli kANisalu idU ondu
kAraNa. tadbhavagaLu badalAvaNe avaSyavendu kANisuva samayadalli
banda padagaLu, mattu tatsamagaLu A avaSyakate illavAdAga eravalAgi
banda padagaLu. Adare I rItiya vayvidhyate ingliSh, hindi




modalAda bhAShegaLinda kannaDakke eravalAgi banda padagaLallU
kANisuttade.

bhASheya varNagaLalli mattu avugaLa vyavastheyalli kAladinda kAlakke
badalAvaNegaLu naDeyuttA iruttave. I badalAvaNegaLu A
bhASheyavE Agiruva padagaLalli mAtravallade, A bhAShege bEre bhAShe
gaLinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLallU naDeyuttave. eravalAgi
bandiruva padagaLalli kANisuva halavu vyatyAsagaLige intaha cAritrika
badalAvaNe innondu mukhya kAraNa.

udAharaNegAgi, kannaDadalli sumAru ondu sAvira varShagaLaShTu
hinde padagaLa Adiyalli baruva pakAra hakAravAguva badalAvaNe
yondu naDeyitu. I badalAvaNeya phalavannu kannaDadavE Ada
padagaLalli mAtravallade, samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva pada
gaLallU kANabahudu.

1. (೧) kannaDada padagaLalli pakAra hakAravAgiruvudu
2. haLegannaDa hosagannaDa
3. pAl hAlu
4. paN haNNu
5. puli huli
6. pO hO(gu)
8. (೨) samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda padagaLalli pakAra hakAra
9. vAgiruvudu
10. samskxta kannaDa
11. pakShi hakki
12. paSu hasu
13. parva habba
14. piShTa hiTTu

idE rItiyalli giDDasvarada anantara baruva rakAravu, adara
anantara vyanjanavondu bandiddAga, A vyanjanadondige sEri ottakShara
vAguva badalAvaNe kannaDadavE Ada padagaLalli mAtravallade samskxta
dinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLallU naDedide.

bhAShegaLalli naDeyuva intaha cAritrika badalAvaNegaLalli prati
yondakkU sAmAnyavAgi ondu avadhiyiruttade. I avadhi dATida
mEle hosadAgi bhASheyoLakke eravalAgi baruva padagaLu A
badalAvaNege oLagAguvudilla. udAharaNegAgi kannaDadalli pakAra
hakAravAguva badalAvaNe hadinAlku-hadinaydanE SatamAnada hottige
pUrNagonDirabEkendu tOruttade. adara anantara samskxtadinda
eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLalli pakAra hAgeyE uLidiruvudannu pakSha,
paTTi, patni, padArtha, pustaka, pUrva modalAda padagaLalli kANa
bahudu. tatsama mattu tadbhava padagaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsakke I rIti
bEre bEre kAlagaLalli samskxtadinda padagaLu eravalAgi bandiruvudu
innondu kAraNa.

bhASheyondannu baLasuva janaru adakke eravalAgi baruva pada
gaLannu bEre bEre vidhAnagaLa mUlaka paDeyuttArembudu A
padagaLalli kANisuva (illavE kANisadiruva) badalAvaNegaLige innondu
kAraNa. udAharaNegAgi, kannaDadalli samskxta padagaLannu baLasuva jana
ralli kelavaru samskxta bhASheyalli cennAgi paLagidavarirabahudu mattu
bEre kelavaru samskxta bhASheya alpa svalpa jYAnaviruvavarirabahudu.
innuLidavarige samskxtada jYAna svalpavU illadirabahudu. samskxta
ballavaru A bhASheya padagaLannu adaralliruvanteyE baLasaballarAdare,
uLidavarige idu sAdhyavAgadu.

eravalAgi banda padagaLu yAva rItiyalli mattu yAva
rUpadalli baLakege baruttave embudu hIge A bhASheyannADuvavarige
eravalAgi padagaLannu koDuva bhASheya jYAna hEgide embudU
AdhAravAgiruttade. idu samskxta mAtravallade ingliSh, hindi
modalAda bhAShegaLigU anvayisuvantaha sangati.

## A.೧.೪ padagaLa vargabhEda




bhASheyondakke eravalAgi baruva padagaLalli heccinavU prANi, vastu,
viShaya modalAduvannu hesarisuvantaha rUDhanAmagaLAgiruttave.
kriyApada illavE guNapadagaLantaha bEre padavargagaLige sErida pada
gaLu I rIti nAmapadagaLa hAge nEravAgi bhASheyondakke eravalAgi
baruvudu kaDime. baruvudiddarU ivu nAmapadagaLa angagaLAgi bandu
anantara bEre padagaLondige baruvAga avugaLinda bErpaTTu
kriyApada illavE guNapadagaLAgi rUDhige baruva sAdhyateyide.

idE rItiyalli padagaLa angagaLAgi baruva pratyayagaLU nEravAgi
ondu bhASheyinda innondu bhAShege eravalAgi baruvudilla. ondu
pratyayavannoLagonDiruva halavAru padagaLu eravalAgi bandalli,
avugaLalliruva pratyaya kAlakramENa A padagaLinda bErpaTTu bhAShe
yavE Ada bEre padagaLondige sEruva mUlaka A bhASheya
pratyayavendenisaballudu.

udAharaNegAgi, samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva naTa-naTi,
lEkhaka-lEkhaki, SikShaka-SikShaki modalAda padayugagaLalli kANisuva a
mattu i emba lingabhEdavannu sUcisuva pratyayagaLa mAdariyalliyE
kannaDada huDuga-huDugi, kuruDa-kuruDi, muduka-muduki
modalAdavugaLalli kANisuva pratyayagaLu tayArAgiruvante tOru
ttade. idE rItiyalli samskxtada dhana-dhanika, rasa-rasika, tarka-
tArkika embantaha padayugagaLalli kANisuva ika emba pratyayavannanu
sarisi, kannaDada gANa-gANiga, heNNu-heNNiga, sAli-sAliga embantaha
padayugagaLalli kANisuva iga emba pratyaya tayArAgiruva hAge
kANisuttade.

Adare, sAmAnyavAgi eravalAgi banda intaha pratyayaviruva
padagaLella itara oLaracaneyillada padagaLa hAge baLakeyAguvudE
jAsti.

## A.೨ eravalAgi banda padagaLa oLaracane

padavondara oLaracane entahadu embudannu nirdharisuvalli sAmAnya
vAgi adannu tayArisuvudakkAgi entaha racaneyannu baLasikoLLalAgittu
emba cAritrika amSakke heccina prAdhAnyateyannu koDabEkAguttade
embudannu nAvu mEle mUraneya adhyAyadalli nODiruvevu.
kriyApada mattu guNapadagaLa oLaracanegintalU nAmapadagaLa oLa
racaneyalli I viShaya eddu kANisuttade. hesarisuvudu mattu varNisu




vudu emba eraDu rItiya baLakegaLige nAmapadagaLu mAtra oLagAgu
ttaveyembudE idakke mukhya kAraNa.


<a id="sec-8-2-1"></a>

## ೮.೨.೧ oLaracaneyalli vyatyAsa

Adare eravalAgi banda padagaLigU mattu bhASheyalliyE beLedu banda
padagaLigU naDuve I viShayadalli ondu mukhyavAda vyatyAsavide.
mEleyE sUcisiruvante, eravalAgi banda padagaLige avugaLannu
eravalAgi koTTiruva bhASheyalli oLaracaneyideyAdarU eravalAgi
paDediruva bhASheyalli avu oLaracaneyillada padagaLa hAge baLakeyAgu
vudE jAsti. udAharaNegAgi, rujuvAtu emba pada parSiyan
bhASheyalli ruju emba padakke vAt emba bahuvacana pratyayavannu
sErisuvudara mUlaka tayArisalAgideyAdarU, kannaDadalli adu
oLaracaneyillada padada hAgeyE baLakeyAguttade. A padakke bahu
vacanArthavU kannaDadallilla.

eravalAgi koDuva bhASheyalli oLaracaneyiruva halavAru pada
gaLu I rIti innondu bhAShege eravalAgi bandiveyAdare, antaha
padagaLa naDuviruva sambandhavannu pariSIlisuvudara mUlaka avakke
oLaracaneyannu eravalu paDeda bhASheyallU kalpisikoLLuva avaSyakate
kANisabahudu. udAharaNegAgi, ingliSh‌ninda AkTar (AkT mADu
vavanu), DAnsar (DAns mADuvavanu), SEvar (SEv mADuva
sAdhana), modalAda halakelavu padagaLu kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiddu,
ivannu AkT, DAns, SEv, modalAda AkhyAta padagaLige ar emba
pratyayavannu sErisuvudara mUlaka tayArAdavugaLendu hELalu sAdhya
vide.

Adare kannaDadalli AkT, DAns, SEv modalAdavugaLu kriyApada
gaLAgi baLakeyallillavAda kAraNa (avu mADu emba kriyApada
dondige 'AkhyAta'padagaLAgi mAtra baLakeyAguvuvAda kAraNa)
inglISh‌nalliruvante kannaDadallU avugaLa oLaracaneyalli kriyApada
gaLiveyendu hELalu sAdhyavAgadu. endare, cAritrikavAgi I padagaLa
tayArikeyalli entaha racaneyannu baLasikoLLalAgittu embudakkintalU
sadyakke I padagaLalli entaha racane kANisuttide embudE illi mukhya
vAda sangati.

idE rItiyalli samskxtadinda kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva
padagaLa oLaracane entahadu embudannu tiLiyalu avu samskxta




dindalEnE eravalAgi bandiruva bEre padagaLondige sambandhagaLannu
tOrisuttiveyE, mattu hAge tOrisuttiveyAdare A sambandhagaLu
entahavu embudE AdhAravAgaballudallade, antaha padagaLannu
eravalAgi koTTiruva samskxta bhASheyalli avakke entaha oLaracane
yide embudu AdhAravAgalAradu.

udAharaNegAgi, kxShNasarpa emba padakke samskxtadalli ondE
vibhaktiyiruva eraDu nAmapadagaLannu (kxShNaH mattu sarpaH embavu
gaLannu) karmadhArayavemba samAsada mUlaka sErisi tayArisiru
vantaha jODupada embudAgi oLaracaneyannu hELalu sAdhyavide.
Adare kannaDadalli I padakke koDabahudAda oLaracane idakkinta tIra
bhinnavAdudu. idakke kAraNavEnendare, kannaDadalli 'kappu' embarthada
kxShNa emba pada guNavAcakavAgi baLakeyallideyallade nAmapadavAgi
baLakeyallilla. samskxtada hAge kannaDadalli adakke vibhakti pratyayagaLannu
sErisalu sAdhyavAgadu. hAgAgi, kannaDada maTTige hELuvudAdare,
kxShNasarpa emba jODupadadalli kxShNa emba ondu guNapadavU
mattu sarpa emba ondu nAmapadavU sErikonDive.

kannaDadalli I rIti ingliSh, samskxta, hindi, marAThi modalAda
halavAru bhAShegaLinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLu baLakeyalliddu
avellavU eravalAgi banda mEle kannaDadavE AgibiTTive. hAgAgi
avugaLa oLaracaneyannu varNisuvAga kannaDadavE Ada padaracaneya
niyamagaLannu anusarisabEkallade I padagaLannu eravalAgi koTTiruva
bEre bEre bhAShegaLalli baLakeyalliruva padaracaneya niyamagaLannu
anusarisuvudu sariyalla. Adare intaha eravalAgi banda padagaLindAgi
kannaDada padaracaneya niyamagaLu bEre bEre rItiyalli badalAgiru
vudannu mattu avugaLondige bEre kelavu hosa padaracaneya
niyamagaLu sErikonDiruvudannu gamanisuvudu avaSya.

## A.೨.೨ eravalu koTTiruva bhASheya niyamagaLu

eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLa mUlaka bhASheyondaralli I rIti
hosatAda padaracaneya niyamagaLu sErikonDiveyAdare, avugaLa
svarUpavEnu embudannu tiLiyalu antaha padagaLa oLaracane eravalu
koTTiruva bhASheyalli hEgittu embudannu tiLiyuvudu svalpa maTTige
sahAyakavAgaballudu.




udAharaNegAgi samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva halavu
padagaLalli ane mattu aNe emba eraDu bEre bEre rUpagaLalliruva
pratyayavondannu kANabahudu. (udA: prArthane-prakaTaNe, varNane-
smaraNe, kalpane-rakShaNe, AlOcane-AkarShaNe, ityAdi). I eraDu
rUpagaLa hindiruva niyamavEnu embudannu tiLiyuvalli samskxtada
vayyAkaraNigaLu I padagaLa oLaracaneyannu hEge vivarisiddAre
embudannu tiLidukonDalli sulabhavAdItu (keLage ೮.೩.೬ nODi).

idE rItiyalli samskxtadindalEnE eravalAgi bandiruva rAjya,
Savrya, vaycitrya modalAda bEre kelavu padagaLalli ya emba
ondu pratyayada baLakeyannu kANabahudu. I pratyaya sEridAga kelavu
padagaLa svaradalli (udA: SUra-Savrya, malina-mAlinya, ityAdi)
badalAvaNeyAguttade, Adare bEre kelavu padagaLa svaradalli (udA:
rAja-rAjya, pada-padya, ityAdi) yAva badalAvaNeyU Aguvudilla.
ika emba pratyayada baLakeyallU idE paristhitiyide (udA: nisarga-
naysargika, mantra-mAntrika, lOka-lavkika, ityAdi). I
badalAvaNe gaLa hindiruva padaracaneya niyamaventahadu embudannu
tiLiyuvalli samskxta vyAkaraNagaLa pariSIlane sahAyakavAgaballudu.

## A.೨.೩ padagaLa vibhajane

eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLa oLaracane entahadu embudannu pari
SIlisuva modalu avannu yAva yAva bhAShegaLinda eravalAgi paDe
yalAgide emba viShayada AdhArada mEle bEre bEre gumpugaLAgi
vingaDisikoLLuvudu avaSya. yAkendare, ondaroDanondu sambandha
vannu tOrisuva padagaLellavU ondE bhASheyinda eravalAgi bandavu
gaLAgiruvudE jAsti.

udAharaNegAgi, samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLu
avugaLoLagEnE ondaroDanondu sambandhisiralu sAdhyavideyallade,
ingliSh illavE parSiyan‌ninda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLondige
sambandhavannu tOrisuvudu bahaLa aparUpavendE hELabahudu.
padagaLa oLaracaneyannu intaha sambandhagaLa AdhArada mEle sAdhisa
bEkAgideyAda kAraNa, eravalu koTTa bhAShegaLa AdhArada mEle
avannu vingaDisikoLLuvudarinda avugaLannu varNisuva kelasa heccu
sulabhavAgaballudu.




keLagina kelavu vibhAgagaLalli (೮.೪-೬ralli) samskxtadinda eravalAgi
bandiruva padagaLige kannaDadalli entaha oLaracaneyide embudannu svalpa
vivaravAgi pariSIlisalAgide. idakke modalu kannaDadalli I padagaLi
giruva oLaracane avakkEnE samskxtadalliruva oLaracaneginta yAke bhinna
vAgide embudannu (೮.೩ralli) svalpa vivaravAgi pariSIlisalAgide.

ingliSh, hindi, marAThi, parSiyan, tamiLu modalAda bEre
halavu bhAShegaLindalU kannaDakke padagaLu eravalAgi badiddu, ivannU
idE rItiyalli bEre bErAgi pariSIlisuva avaSyakateyide. Adare
antaha prayatnavannu I pustakakkAgi naDesalu sAdhyavAgalilla.


<a id="sec-8-3"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#sec-8-3)

## ೮.೩ samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda padagaLu

kannaDadalli samskxtadinda eravalAgi banda padagaLu halavive. ivugaLa
sankhye kannaDada bEre bEre prabhEdagaLalli bEre bErAgide. SAstrIya
barahagaLalli intaha padagaLu jAsti ive Adare bEre rItiya baraha
gaLalli kaDime ive. eravalAgi banda I padagaLa svarUpavU prabhEda
dinda prabhEdakke bhinna bhinnavAgide. kelavu prabhEdagaLalli ivu mUla
samskxta rUpadallE uLidiveyAdare, innu kelavu prabhEdagaLalli
halavAru badalAvaNegaLige oLagAguvudara mUlaka mUla samskxta
padagaLiginta tIra bhinnavAgive.

samskxtadinda kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLellavU samskxta
dalli oLaracaneyuLLavugaLE Agiruttaveyendu hELabahudu. avellakkU
mUladalli bEre bEre kriyAdhAtugaLE AdhAravAgiddu, A dhAtugaLige
bEre bEre pratyayagaLannu illavE itara dhAtugaLannu sErisuvudara
mUlaka samskxtadalli I padagaLannu racisalAgide.

Adare kannaDada maTTige ivugaLalli kelavannu mAtra oLaracaneyiru
vavugaLendu parigaNisalu sAdhyavide. yAkendare, I rIti eravalAgi
bandiruva padavondakke oLaracaneyideyendu hELabEkAdare, kannaDa
dallE bEre padagaLondige adu rUpa mattu arthagaLalli sambandha
vannu tOrisuttiruvudu avaSya.

I kAraNakkAgi eravalAgi bandiruva ondu padakke oLaracane
yideyE athavA illavE embudu nAvu pariSIlisuttiruva kannaDada
prabhEdavannanusarisi bEre bErAgiralu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi, satya
emba padakke kelavu prabhEdagaLalli oLaracaneyilla endu hELalu sAdhya
vide, Adare bEre kelavu prabhEdagaLalli (endare sat emba padavannU




eravalAgi paDediddu, adakke ya emba pratyayavannu sErisuvudara
mUlaka satya emba padavannu tayArisalu sAdhyaviruvantaha prabhEda
dalli) adakke oLaracaneyideyendU vAdisalu sAdhyavAdItu. samskxta
dinda jAsti padagaLannu eravalAgi paDediruva kannaDada prabhEdagaLalli
jAsti padagaLige oLaracaneyideyendu parigaNisalu sAdhya emba viShaya
idarinda spaShTavAguttade.

hIgiddarU mEle sUcisidante, eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLa oLa
racane avakke mUla bhASheyalli (endare samskxtadalli) iruva oLa
racaneginta tIra bhinnavAgiralu sAdhyavideyAda kAraNa, kannaDada
vyAkaraNadalli avannu pratyEkavAgi pariSIlisuvudu avaSya, mattu
antaha pariSIlaneya AdhArada mEle avakke kannaDadavE Ada pada
racaneya niyamagaLannu tayArisikoLLuvudu avaSya.

samskxtada vayyAkaraNigaLu koDuva padaracaneya niyamagaLannu
hAgeyE kannaDada vyAkaraNadoLage tandu hAkidalli avu I eravalAgi
banda padagaLa oLaracaneyannu sariyAgi tiLisihELalAravu. kannaDa mattu
samskxta vyAkaraNagaLa naDuve halavAru prAmukhyavAda vyatyAsagaLiddu,
eravalAgi banda padagaLu kannaDada vyAkaraNa niyamagaLannanusarisuvudE
hIge mADalu sAdhyavAgadiruvudakke mukhya kAraNa.

samskxta mattu kannaDa vyAkaraNagaLa naDuve padaracanege sambandhisi
dantaha vyatyAsagaLalli prAmukhyavAda kelavannu keLagina vibhAgagaLalli
paricayisalAgide. samskxdadinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLa oLa
racane kannaDadalli samskxtadalliruvudakkinta yAke bhinnavAgide mattu
yAva rItiyalli bhinnavAgide embudannu tiLiyalu I vyatyAsagaLa
arivu sahAyakavAgaballudu.

## A.kha.೧ padavargadalli vyatyAsa

kannaDadalli nAmapada, kriyApada mattu guNapadagaLembudAgi mUru
mukhyavAda padavargagaLiveyendU mattu ivugaLalli guNapadagaLu
nAmapadagaLondige sErihOguvuvAda kAraNa samskxtadalli nAmapada
mattu kriyApadagaLemba eraDu mukhya padavargagaLu mAtra ive
yendU nAvu eraDaneya adhyAyadalli nODiruvevu.

samskxtakkU mattu kannaDakkU naDuviruva I vyatyAsada pariNAma
vAgi, samskxtadinda kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLalli halavakke




samskxtadalli kANisuva oLaracaneginta bhinnavAda oLaracaneyannu kalpisi
koDuva avaSyakate kanDubaruttade.

samskxtadinda kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLalli heccinavU
nAmapadagaLE. avugaLalli kelavu guNapadagaLAgiyU mattu bEre
kelavu nAmapadagaLAgiyU kannaDadalli baLakeyAguttave. udAharaNe
gAgi, nIli, bEga (vEga), mukhya, uttama, yOgya modalAda
samskxtada nAmapadagaLu kannaDadalli guNapadagaLAgiyU mattu grAma,
kavi, pATha, vidye, sEvaka, yantra modalAda nAmapadagaLu
kannaDadalli nAmapadagaLAgiyU baLakeyAguttave.

samskxtada kriyApadagaLu nEravAgi kriyApadagaLAgiyE kannaDakke
eravalAgi baruvudilla. idakke badalu avu bhUtakxdanta (sambandhaka)
rUpadalli guNapadagaLAgi nAmapadagaLondige (udA: dxDha manassu,
gupta jIvana, bhagna kanasu, SAnta cahare, ityAdi), illavE iru
emba kriyApadadondige (udA: dxDhavAgu, guptavAgu, SAnta
vAgu, hitavAgu, ityAdi) baruttave.

samskxtadalli nAmapada mattu kriyApadagaLemba eraDu mukhya pada
vargagaLu mAtravallade, avyayavemba innondu amukhya padavargavU
ide. I padavargakke sErida padagaLU kannaDakke guNapadagaLAgi
eravalAguttave. (udA: punaH, vxthA, nAnA, ityAdi).

samskxtadinda kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLa oLaracane
yemhadembudannu nirdharisuvallU padavargagaLa maTTige ivugaLa
naDuve kANisuva I vyatyAsavannu parigaNisuva avaSyakateyide. idannu
mukhyavAgi jODupadagaLa oLaracaneyalli kANabahudu. samskxtada
jODupadagaLige tatpuruSha, karmadhAraya, dvigu, dvandva, bahuvrIhi
mattu avyayibhAvagaLemba Aru mukhyavAda oLaracane (samAsa)gaLannu
kalpisikoLLuva avaSyakateyideyendu samskxtada vayyAkaraNigaLu abhi
prAyapaTTiddAre. Adare kannaDada jODupadagaLige idakkinta tIra bhinna
vAda oLaracanegaLannu kalpisikoLLuva avaSyakateyideyembudannu nAvu
mEle Araneya adhyAyadalli nODiddEve.

kannaDada jODupadagaLige mAtravallade samskxtadinda eravalAgi
bandiruva jODupadagaLigU kannaDadalli samskxtada Aru oLaracane
(samAsa)gaLiginta bhinnavAgiruva oLaracanegaLannu kalpisikoLLuva avaSyakate
yide. udAharaNegAgi, samskxtadalli tatpuruSha mattu karmadhAraya
gaLemba eraDu rItiya jODupadagaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsavEnendare,




tatpuruShadalli oTTu sEruva nAmapadagaLu bEre bEre vibhaktigaLalliru
ttave (rAjYaH 'rAjana' puruShaH 'jana' rAjapuruShaH), mattu karma
dhArayadalli oTTusEruva nAmapadagaLu ondE vibhaktiyalliruttave
(kxShNaH 'kappu' sarpaH 'hAvu' kxShNasarpaH).

Adare kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva intaha jODupadagaLalli
karmadhAraya samAsavannu tOrisuva halavu padagaLige kannaDadalli
bEreyE ondu oLaracaneyannu kalpisikoDabEkAguttade. yAkendare,
vibhaktiyondige baralArada guNapadadondige nAmapadavondannu
sErisuvantaha oLaracane ivugaLigide. mEle koTTiruva kxShNasarpa
emba pada mAtravallade, paramAnna, sadguNa, mandabuddhi, mUla
dhana, SuklapakSha modalAdavugaLU kannaDadalli intaha oLaracaneyannu
tOrisuttave.

## A.vi.೨ pUrva mattu parapratyayagaLu

samskxtadalli baLakeyalliruva padagaLalli heccinavannU (kelavara abhi
prAyadante ellA padagaLannU) kriyApadavemba ondE ondu pada
vargakke sErida dhAtugaLinda tayArisalAgide. bahuSaH idE kAraNakkAgi
samskxtada padagaLalli kANisikoLLuva pratyayagaLa sankhye bahaLa
doDDadu. I pratyayagaLu dhAtuvina eDakke sEruvuvAdare avannu
pUrvapratyaya (illavE upasarga)gaLendU mattu balakke sEruvu
vAdare avannu parapratyayagaLendU kareyuvudu rUDhi.

vidyArthi vidyArthini

kannaDadalli nAma, kriye mattu guNagaLemba mUru bEre bEre
padavargagaLige sEruva dhAtugaLiveyAda kAraNa adakke aShTondu
pratyayagaLa avaSyakateyillavendu hELalu sAdhyavide. idallade
kannaDadalli parapratyayagaLu mAtra iveyallade pUrvapratyayagaLilla. I
kAraNakkAgi samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLalli
pUrvapratyayaviruvavu gaLu kannaDadalli bEre bEre rItiya
oLaracanegaLannu tOrisuttave.

intaha padagaLalli kelavannu kannaDadalli jODupadagaLendu kareyu
vudE oLLeyadendu tOruttade. ivu kannaDadalli guNapada mattu nAma
padagaLannu oTTu sErisi racisida jODupadagaLa hAge kANisuvudE
idakke mukhya kAraNa. udAharaNegAgi, samskxtada ati emba pUrva
pratyaya kannaDadalli ati doDDa, atiyAgi modalAda kaDegaLalli guNa
padada hAge svatantravAgi baLakeyAguttade. hAgAgi, atikramaNa,
atyAsa, atyanta modalAdavugaLalli samskxtadalliruvante pada
vondakke pUrva pratyaya sErideyendu hELuva badalu, guNapada
vondakke nAmapada sEri jODupadavAgideyendu hELuvudE kannaDada
maTTige heccu sari.

idE rItiyalli prati emba pUrvapratyayavU kannaDadalli ondu
svatantravAda padavAgi baLakeyalliddu (udA: pratiyAgi, pratiyobba),
adarondige baruva padagaLannU jODupadagaLendu kareyalu sAdhya
vide. I rIti svatantravAgi baradiddarU padagaLa hAge mukhyavAda
arthavannE koDaballa upa, dur, sva modalAdavugaLannU kannaDadalli
asvatantra padagaLendu kareyalu sAdhyaviddu, avannoLagonDiruva pada
gaLannU kannaDadalli samskxtada hAge pUrvapratyayagaLiruva padagaLendu
hELade, jODupadagaLendu hELalu sAdhyavide. udA:

prati kriye pratikriye
sthApane pratisthApane
dhvani pratidhvani
pAlane pratipAlane
kxti pratikxti

Adare itara kelavu eravalAgi banda padagaLannu pUrvapratyaya
viruva padagaLendu hELuvudE oLLeyadendu tOruttade. udAharaNe
gAgi, prakhyAta, prayatna, modalAduvannu khyAta, yatna modalAda
vugaLondige hOlisi nODidAga avugaLa modalaneya angavAda pra
embudu ondu pUrvapratyayavAgi kANisikoLLuttade. idE rItiyalli,
vikhyAta, vivAda, vijYAna, vinASa, viyOga modalAdavugaLannu
khyAta, vAda, jYAna, nASa modalAdavugaLondige hOlisi
nODidAga, avugaLallU vi emba modalaneya anga pUrvapratyaya
vAgi kANisikoLLuttade. kannaDadalli ivannu svatantra illavE asvatantra
padagaLendu hELuvudu kaShTavAda kAraNa ivugaLindAgi kannaDadallillada
pUrvapratyayagaLu eravalinindAgi bandiveyendu hELabEkAguttade.

## A.kha.kha dhAtugaLalli vyatyAsa

mEleyE sUcisiruvante, samskxtadalli baLakeyAguva padagaLellavU
oLaracaneyuLLavugaLE Agiddu, avannella ondalla ondu kriyAdhAtu
vininda sAdhisalu sAdhya embudAgi vayyAkaraNigaLu abhiprAyapaTTi




ddAre. idakke vyatiriktavAgi, kannaDadalli oLaracaneyilladantaha halavAru
nAmapada, kriyApada mattu guNapadagaLu baLakeyallive. hAgAgi,
samskxtadalli 'dhAtu' emba pada 'kriyAdhAtu' emba ondu arthadalli
mAtra baLakeyAgaballudAdare, kannaDadalli nAmadhAtu, kriyAdhAtu
mattu guNadhAtu embudAgi mUru bEre bEre arthagaLalli
baLakeyAgaballudu.

samskxtada padaracaneyalli baLakeyAguva pratyayagaLannu mukhyavAgi
eraDu vargagaLalli vingaDisuva kramavide. nEravAgi kriyAdhAtuga
Londige baruva pratyayagaLannu kxt pratyayagaLendU mattu antaha
pratyayagaLannu sErisi tayArisida padagaLondige baruva pratyayagaLannu
taddita pratyayagaLendU kareyuvudu rUDhi. udAharaNegAgi, dhan
emba kriyAdhAtuvininda dhana emba nAmapadavannu tayArisalu
baLasuva a emba pratyaya ondu kxt‌pratyaya mattu dhana emba A
nAmapadadinda dhanavat (dhanavAn) emba bErondu nAmapadavannu
tayArisalu baLasuva vat emba pratyaya ondu taddita pratyaya.

idallade upasargagaLemba pUrvapratyayagaLU samskxta padagaLa
tayArikeyalli baLakeyAguttave. ivu kxt mattu taddhita pratyayagaLa
hAge padagaLa anantara (balakke) baruva badalu avugaLa modalige
(eDakke) baruttave. udAharaNegAgi, jYAna emba padakke a emba
upasargavannu sErisi ajYAna emba padavannU, svapna emba padakke
dur emba upasargavannu sErisi dusvapna emba padavannU mattu
jIvana emba padakke upa emba upasargavannu sErisi upajIvana
emba padavannU tayArisabahudu.

kannaDada vayyAkaraNigaLu samskxtada I vidhAnavannE anusarisi
kannaDadavE Ada padagaLa oLaracaneyannu kxt‌pratyaya mattu taddhita
pratyayagaLemba eraDu rItiya pratyayagaLa sahAyadinda varNisalu
prayatnisiddAre. Adare I prayatna kannaDa padagaLa maTTige yaSasviyAga
lAradu. yAkendare, kannaDadalli nAmadhAtu, kriyAdhAtu mattu
guNadhAtu embudAgi mUru rItiya dhAtugaLiddu, kannaDada padagaLannu
I mUru rItiya dhAtugaLige bEre bEre rItiya pratyayagaLannu
sErisuvudara mUlaka sAdhisabEkAguttade.

samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLannU kannaDadavE Ada
oLaracaneya vidhAnagaLa mUlaka varNisabEkAguttadallade samskxta
vyAkaraNagaLalli baLakeyalliruva vidhAnagaLa mUlaka varNisalu sAdhya




vAgadu. yAkendare, mEle (೮.೩)ralli sUcisidante I padagaLa
oLaracane mukhyavAgi avakkU kannaDadalli baLakeyalliruva itara pada
gaLigU naDuviruva sambandhada mEle Adharisiruttadeyallade samskxta
dalli I padagaLigiruva oLaracaneya AdhArada mElalla.

udAharaNegAgi kannaDakke samskxtadinda kriyApadagaLu nEravAgi
eravalAguvudilla. avugaLondige kxt illavE taddita pratyayagaLu
sEriruva rUpadallAgali, illavE kannaDada isu emba pratyaya
dondigAgali avu baLakege baruttave (udA: rakShaNe-rakShisu, ASraya-
ASrita-ASrayisu, ityAdi). hAgAgi, kannaDakke samskxtadinda eravalAgi
bandiruva padagaLa oLaracaneyannu sandarbhakkanusAravAgi kelavu
asvatantravAda dhAtugaLannu kalpisuvudara mUlaka varNisabEkAguttade.
heccinaDegaLallU I dhAtugaLu yAva vargakke sEruttave embudannu
nirdharisalu kannaDadalli yAva AdhAravU doreyuvudilla (೮.೫
nODi).

## A.vi.A tayArike mattu baLake

kannaDa mattu samskxta padagaLa naDuve innondu prAmukhyavAda
vyatyAsavide. kannaDada nAmapadagaLige tayArike mattu baLake embudAgi
eraDu bhinna bhinnavAda avasthegaLiddu, I padagaLu yAvudAdarondu
sandarbhadalli tayArAda baLika, baLakege bandu uLidare mAtra bhASheya
padagaLendenisaballuvu (೧.೬.೧ nODi). I kAraNakkAgi, oLaracaneya
maTTige 'niyamabaddha'vAgi kANisuva pratyayaviruva nAmapada illavE
jODupadagaLellavU kannaDadalli bhASheya padagaLAguvudilla. antaha
padagaLu ondu niScitavAda arthadalli rUDhige bandAga mAtra avu
bhASheya padagaLendenisaballuvu.

idallade, bhASheyalli rUDhige bandiruva kannaDada padagaLu oLa
racaneya maTTige 'niyamabaddha'vAgi illadiralU sAdhyavide. padakkondu
niyama ennuvaShTara maTTige kannaDadalli pratyayaviruva padagaLa mattu
jODupadagaLa oLaracane aniyamitavAgiralu sAdhyavide. idakke kAraNa
vEnEndare, kannaDa bhASheya nijavAda svarUpa mAtina baLakeyallEnE
siddhavAguvantahadu. barahadalli adannu baLasuttiruvevAdarU, mAti
giruvaShTu mahatva barahakkilla. kaLeda ondUvare-eraDu sAvira varSha
gaLalli kannaDa bhAShe eShTondu badalAvaNegaLigoLagAgide (pUrvada
haLegannaDaviddudu haLegannaDavAgi, naDugannaDavAgi anantara hosagannaDa




vAgide mattu hosagannaDadallU UrindUrige mattu jAtiyinda
jAtige adu bhinna bhinnavAgide) embudannu pariSIlisidevAdare mAtina
baLakege I bhASheya svarUpavannu nirdharisuvalli entaha mahatvavide
emba viShaya spaShTavAdItu.

I kAraNakkAgi, kannaDada vyAkaraNa niyamagaLannu racisuvavaru adu
barahadalli mAtravallade mAtinallU yAva rUpadallide embudannu
gamanisuvudu avaSya. innondu prAmukhyavAda sangatiyEnendare,
barahagaLu bhASheya ondu cikka amSavannu mAtravE pratinidhIkarisa
balluvu. udAharaNegAgi, tinnu emba kriyApadakkiruva halavu rUpa
gaLalli (tinnuttAne, tinda, tinnali, tinnuttEne, tinnaliddEne,
tinnuttiddALe, ityAdi) kelavE kelavannu mAtra barahagaLalli kANa
ballevu. uLida rUpagaLannu paDeyalu mAtina marehogabEkAguttade.

idallade bhAShe mAtinalli badalAdante barahadallU badalAgu
ttiddu, I viShayadalli baraha mAtannanusarisuvudallade, mAtu baraha
vannanusarisuvudilla. kAladinda kAlakke barahada bhASheyalli badalAvaNe
gaLunTAgalu adakke modalu mAtinalli badalAvaNegaLunTAgiruvudE
mukhya kAraNavAgiruttade.

I viShayadalli samskxta bhAShe kannaDakkinta (mattu sAvirAru itara
bhAShegaLiginta) bahaLa maTTige bhinnavAgide. kaLeda eraDu sAvira varSha
gaLalli (pANiniya kAladindIcege) samskxta bhAShe svalpavU badalAgade
hAgeyE uLidide. I dIrghavAda avadhiyalli adara prayOgagaLigella
barahada bhAShe mUlAdhAravAgiddudE idakke mukhya kAraNa. eraDu
sAvira varShagaLaShTu hinde racitavAgidda pANiniya vyAkaraNa niyama
gaLu ivattigU A bhASheyalli padagaLannu mattu padarUpagaLannu
tayArisalu AdhAravAgiruttave. I niyamagaLannu mIruva padagaLu
illavE padarUpagaLu sAdhuvenisabEkAdare, avu mahAkavigaLa illavE
vidvAmsara barahagaLalli kANisabEku, endare mAnyavAda barahagaLalli
rUDhige bandirabEku.

pANiniya kAlada samskxtadalli padagaLa tayArike mattu baLake
gaLemba eraDu ghaTTagaLa naDuve spaShTavAda vyatyAsavittu. Atana vyAkaraNa
dalli onderaDu padagaLa racanege mAtravE anvayisuvantaha niyama
gaLU halaviveyembudu I viShayavannu spaShTapaDisuttave. Adare Atana
kAlada anantarada kAladalli samskxta bhAShe bariya barahada bhASheyAgi
uLidu, adakke mAtina baLakeya AdhAra tappihOyitu.




mAtinalli A bhAShe pAli, prAkxta, apabhramSa ityAdiyAgi
badalAguttA hOdarU barahadalli mAtra antaha badalAvaNegaLannu
anusarisade iddudiddanteyE uLidukonDudE idakke kAraNa. endare,
kannaDa baraha haLegannaDaviddaddu naDugannaDavAgi anantara hosagannaDavAgi
badalAgide, Adare samskxta baraha samskxtaviddaddu prAkxtavAgi
anantara hindi, marAThi modalAdavugaLalli ondAgalilla, idakke badalu
adu samskxtavAgiyE uLidukonDide.

bhASheya maTTige hIge kAladinda kAlakke badalAgade uLiyuvudu
ondu asvAbhAvika ghaTaneyendu hELabahudu. I kAraNakkAgi
samskxtada vyAkaraNavU kelavu asvAbhAvika guNadharmagaLannu tOrisu
ide. adara nAmapadagaLalli tayArike mattu baLake emba I eraDu
ghaTTagaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsa heccina maTTige illavAgiruvudu intaha
guNadharmagaLalli prAmukhyavAdudu. kannaDa mattu samskxta bhAShegaLa
naDuve I viShayadalli bahaLa spaShTavAda vyatyAsavide. idannu I eraDu
bhAShegaLalli baLakeyAguva jODupadagaLa pariSIlaneyinda tiLidukoLLa
bahudu.

kannaDadalli jODupadagaLannu tayArisida kUDalE avu bhASheya
padagaLAguvudilla. hAge tayArisida padagaLu idakkAgi bhASheyalli
rUDhige baruva avaSyakateyide. udAharaNegAgi, eraDu
nAmapadagaLannu oTTige sErisi tayArisiruva bayalATa, neligaDale,
jEnuhuLa, tAyimane modalAda jODupadagaLannu
gamanisabahudu. bayalina ATa, nelada kaDale, jEnina huLa,
tAyiya mane modalAda padagucchagaLalli modalaneya padadondige
bandiruva a emba sambandhaka pratyayavannu tegedu hAki I
jODupadagaLannu tayArisa lAgide.

Adare ellA rItiya padagucchagaLindalU I rIti modalaneya
padadondige baruva sambandhaka pratyayavannu tegedu hAki avannu
kannaDada jODupadagaLendu kareyalu sAdhyavAgadu. udAharaNegAgi
bayalina OTa, nelada baNNa, marada huLa, tAyiya sIre,
modalAda padagucchagaLinda avugaLa modalaneya padadondige baruva
sambandhaka pratyayavannu tegedu hAki bayalOTa, nelabaNNa,
marahuLa, tAyisIre embudAgi padagaLannu tayArisalu
sAdhyavideyadarU avu nijakkU kannaDada jODupadagaLalla. antaha
padagaLannu nAvu kannaDada arthakOSagaLalli kANuvudU illa.




bayalATa, nelagaDale modalA davugaLa hAge avakkondu
viSiShTavAda artha dorakida mEle mattu A arthadalli avu
bhASheyalli baLakege banda mEle mAtravE avannu kannaDada
jODupadagaLendu hELalu mattu kannaDada arthakOSagaLalli avannu
sErisikoLLalu sAdhyavAdItu.

kriyApadagaLondige nAmapadagaLannu sErisi tayArisiruva jAru
banDi, cuccumaddu, hurigaDale, biccugatti, huTTuhabba modalAda
jODupadagaLa baLakeyU idE rItiyadu. sAmAnyavAgi kriyApada
vondannu nAmapadadondige baLasabEkiddalli adannu sambandhaka rUpa
dallirisabEku. jAruva nela, cuccuva muLLu, biccida kUdalu,
huTTida rAtri modalAda padagucchagaLalli intaha racaneyannu kANa
bahudu. intaha padagucchagaLalli jAruva banDi, cuccuva maddu,
hurida kaDale modalAda kelavu padagucchagaLu mAtra avugaLa
modalaneya padadondige bandiruva kAlapratyaya mattu sambandhaka
pratyayagaLannu kaLedukonDu jODupadagaLAgi kannaDadalli baLakege
bandive.

jAruva nela, cuccuva muLLu modalAda itara padaguccha
gaLindalU jAruneli, cuccumuLLu modalAda intaha jODupada
gaLannu tayArisalu sAdhyavideyAdarU avu kannaDada jODupadagaLu
endenisabEkiddalli avakke mEle hELidante viSiShTavAdondu artha
sigabEku mattu A arthadalli avu baLakege barabEku.

guNapadagaLondige nAmapadagaLannu sErisi tayArisiruva
doDDaNNa, aDDadAri, beNkallu modalAda jODupadagaLa baLake
idakkinta svalpa bhinnavAgideyAdarU tayArike mattu baLakegaLa
naDuviruva antara illU spaShTavAgiyE kANisikoLLuttade. kannaDadalli
guNapadagaLannu nEravAgi nAmapadagaLondige baLasalu sAdhyavide. Adare
intaha baLakegaLu bariya padagucchagaLAgiruttavallade
jODupadagaLendenisuvu dilla. udAharaNegAgi, doDDa mane,
aDDagODe, biLikallu modalA davugaLu bariya padagucchagaLu mAtra.

ivu kannaDadalli jODupadagaLendenisabEkAdare, mEle hELidante
ivakkU ondu viSiShTavAda artha labhisabEku mattu A arthadalli avu
baLakege barabEku. Adare I rIti padagucchagaLu jODupadagaLAgi
badalAguvAga ivugaLalli pratyayagaLAvuvU bidduhOguvudilla (ivu
gaLalli bidduhOguvantaha pratyayagaLE illa) embudE ivugaLigU




mattu mEle koTTiruva bEre eraDu rItiya jODupadagaLigU
naDuviruva vyatyAsa. Adare intaha guNapadagaLiruva jODupadagaLalli
sAmAnyavAgi padagucchagaLalli kANisadiruva kelavu sandhiya niyama
gaLannu kANabahudu (udA: biLi-beL, kappu-kari, kar ityAdi).

samskxtadalli kANisuva jODupadagaLa baLake idakkinta tIra bhinna
vAdudu. adara kelavu jODupadagaLige padagucchagaLiginta bhinnavAda
artha ideyAdarU, avannu antaha arthadalli mAtravallade bariya
padagucchada arthadallU baLasalu sAdhyavide. nijakkU 'samAsa'vemba
vyAkaraNa vidhAna samskxtadalli eraDu athavA jAsti nAmapadagaLannu
oTTige sankShipta rUpadalli baLasuva ondu sAdhana mAtra. adannondu
padaracaneya vidhAnavannunnuvudakkintalU vAkyavannu sankShiptagoLisuva
sAdhanavendu hELuvudE heccu samanjasavAgaballudu.

sandhikAryagaLa mUlaka padagaLa naDuve baruva akSharagaLannu tegedu
hAki illavE badalAyisi A padagaLu ondaroDanondu jODikoLLu
vante mADuva hAgeyE samskxtadalli samAsa kAryagaLa mUlaka
padagaLa naDuve baruva linga-vacana-vibhakti pratyayagaLannu tegedu hAki
avu innaShTu hattira bandu jODikoLLuvante mADalu sAdhyavAguttade.
I eraDu vyAkaraNa kriyegaLallU samskxtadalli padagaLa ananyate naShTa
vAguvudilla. samskxtada I samAsa vidhAna kannaDadalli kANisuva
samAsa vidhAnadinda tIra bhinnavAdudu.

samskxtada jODupadagaLa baLakeyalli tayArike mattu baLake emba
eraDu ghaTTagaLilla emba viShaya bANabhaTTana kAdambariyalli kANisi
koLLuva jODupadagaLannu pariSIlisidalli bahaLa spaShTavAgaballudu.
ippattu-mUvattu padagaLannu oTTusErisi tayArisida udduddavAda
jODupadagaLu halavu A granthadallive. intaha jODupadagaLige
tayArikeyemba ondE ondu ghaTTaviralu sAdhyavideyallade adakkinta
bhinnavAda baLakeyemba eraDaneya ghaTTaviruvudu asAdhya. yAkendare
antaha udduddavAgiruva jODupadagaLannu punaH punaH baLasuva
sandarbhagaLE baralAravu.

samskxta bhASheyalli I rIti hosa hosa padagaLannu tayArisi
hELalu mAtina baLakeya AdhAra bEkAgillavAda kAraNa, mattu antaha
padagaLige artha hELalu avugaLa oLaracane mAtravE AdhAravAgiralu
sAdhyavideyAda kAraNa, kannaDadalli hosa hosa pAribhAShika padagaLannu
baLasabEkAgiruva sandarbhagaLallella samskxta bhAShege marehoguva krama




rUDhige bandide. (ingliSh‌nallU idE rItiyalli hosa hosa
pAribhAShika padagaLannu baLasabEkAdAgalella lyATin illavE grIk
bhAShege mare hoguva krama rUDhiyallittembudannu illi gamanisa
bahudu.) pAribhAShika padagaLige avugaLa oLaracaneyindalEnE nEra
vAgi artha siguvantiddare oLLeyademba anisikeyE hIge mADalu
ondu kAraNavirabEku.

sumAru eraDu sAvira varShagaLaShTu dIrghavAda avadhiyalli
samskxta bhAShe mAtina baLakeya AdhAra tappihOgi bariya barahada
baLakeya AdhArada mEle mattu vidvAmsaru racisida vyAkaraNa niyama
gaLa AdhArada mEle mAtravE nillabEkAgi bandide. I kAraNakkAgi I
bhAShe harivu ninta nIrina hAge jaDavAgide mattu tanna jIvantikeyannu
bahaLa maTTige kaLedukonDide. adara vyAkaraNada halavu bhAgagaLalli
idarindAgi kxtakate eddu kANisuttade. mEle vivarisidante tayArike
mattu baLakegaLemba eraDu ghaTTagaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsa adara nAma
padagaLa baLakeyalli kANisadiruvudu intaha kxtakatege ondu udA
haraNe.

kelavaru vidvAmsaru samskxtada I kxtakate A bhAShe itara illA
bhAShegaLigintalU 'SrEShTha'vAgiruvudara dyOtakavendu bhramisidantide.
udAharaNegAgi samskxtavannu itara bhAShegaLiginta heccu sulabhavAgi
kampyUTar‌nalli aLavaDisikoLLalu sAdhyavAguttadeyemba viShayavannu
pariSIlisabahudu. samskxtada vyAkaraNavannu vivaravAgi mattu vistAra
vAgi varNisalAgideyembudu idakke ondu kAraNavAdare, samskxtada
nAmapadagaLalli heccinavakkU avugaLa oLaracaneya AdhArada mEle
artha hELalu sAdhya embudu innondu kAraNa. ivugaLalli eraDane
yadu A bhASheya SrEShThateyannu tOrisuva badalu adara jaDatvavannu
(illavE jIvantikeya abhAvavannu) tOrisuttade.

## A.೪ pratyayaviruva padagaLu

mEleyE sUcisiruvante, samskxtadinda kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva
padagaLige oLaracaneyideyE athavA illavE embudannu, mattu
ideyAdare adu entahadu embudannu mukhyavAgi I rIti
eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLa naDuviruva sambandhaventahadu emba
viShayada AdhArada mEle nirdharisabEkAguttade. A padagaLige samskxta




vyAkaraNadalli koTTiruva oLaracanegaLannu hAgeyE nEravAgi kannaDada
vyAkaraNadalli tandu sErisuvudu sulabhavAdarU adu sariyalla.

samskxtadalli heccu kaDime ellA nAmapadagaLannU kriyAdhAtugaLige
pratyayagaLannu sErisuvudara mUlaka, illavE eraDu athavA jAsti
nAmapadagaLannu oTTige sErisi jODupadagaLannu racisuvudara mUlaka
tayArisalAgide. Adare samskxtadinda kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva
nAmapadagaLalli halavu kannaDada maTTige oLaracaneyillada padagaLendE
hELabEkAguttade. avugaLondige sambandhavannu tOrisuva bEre
samskxta padagaLu kannaDakke eravalAgi bandillavembudE idakke kAraNa.

udAharaNegAgi, anna emba nAmapadavannu samskxtadalli 'tinnu'
emba arthadalliruva ad emba kriyAdhAtuvige kxt‌pratyayavondannu
sErisuvudara mUlaka tayArisalAgide. Adare, kannaDakke I ad emba
kriyApada samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandillavAda kAraNa (೮.೫ nODi),
anna embudakke kannaDadalli oLaracaneyillavendE hELabEkAguttade.
idE rItiyalli kShI emba dhAtuvininda tayArAda kShINa emba nAma
pada, nad emba dhAtuvininda tayArAda nadi emba nAmapada,
muh emba dhAtuvininda tayArAda mUDha emba nAmapada, Sudh
emba dhAtuvininda tayArAda Suddha emba nAmapada, modalAdavu
gaLigU kannaDadalli oLaracaneyideyendu hELalu AdhAra kANisuvudilla.

## A.೪.೧ pUrvapratyayagaLu

samskxtadalli pUrvapratyaya (upasarga) mattu parapratyayagaLemba
eraDu rItiya pratyayagaLannoLagonDiruva padagaLiddu, kannaDakke
samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLallU I eraDu rItiya
pratyayagaLannu kANabahudu. Adare mEle (೮.೩.೨ralli) sUcisiru
vante, kannaDadavE Ada padagaLalli pUrvapratyayagaLa baLakeyillavAda
kAraNa, samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva I padagaLallU kelavu
pUrva pratyayagaLu svatantra illavE asvatantra padagaLa hAge baLakege
bandive, mattu antaha pratyayagaLannoLagonDiruva padagaLu jODu
padagaLa hAge kANisuttave.

Adare bEre kelavu pUrvapratyayagaLu pratyayagaLa hAgeyE
vartisuttiddu, avannoLagonDiruva padagaLannu pratyayaviruva pada
gaLendu hELalu sAdhyavide. intaha pUrvapratyayagaLalli a, nir, vi,
sam mattu su embavugaLu mukhyavAdavugaLu.




1. (೧) a pratyaya
2. I pratyayavannu ondu nAmapadadondige baLasidAga, A padada
3. viruddhArtha siguttade. idakke svaradalli prArambhavAguva padagaLeduru

## A.೪.೨ parapratyayagaLu

samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva nAmapadagaLalli kANisuva para
pratyayagaLalli te, i, ya mattu ika embavugaLu prAmukhyavAdavu
gaLu. idallade lingabhEdavannu sUcisuva kelavu pratyayagaLU samskxta
dinda eravalAgi banda padagaLalli kANisuttave. I pratyayagaLalli
kelavannu (prAmukhyavAgi ya mattu ika emba pratyayagaLannu)
baLasidAga padagaLalli kelavu badalAvaNegaLAguttave. I badalAvaNe
gaLannu keLage (೮.೪.೩ralli) vivarisalAgide.

## (೧) te pratyaya

1. (೧) ta pratyaya
2. I pratyayada mUlaka nAmapadagaLu hesarisuva vyakti, vastu modalA
3. davugaLa guNadharmavannu hesarisuvantaha bErondu nAmapadavannu
4. tayArisabahudu. udA:
6. adhyakSha adhyakShate
7. kxtajYa kxtajYate
8. arha arhate
9. aspxSya aspxSyate
10. yOgya yOgyate
11. tIkShNa tIkShNate
13. (೨) i pratyaya
14. I pratyayakke eraDu rItiya baLakegaLiveyendu (illavE i emba
15. rUpadalliruva eraDu bEre bEre pratyayagaLiveyendu) hELalu
16. sAdhyavide. I eraDu baLakegaLallU idu akAradalli konegoLLuva
17. nAmapadadondige avugaLa koneya akArakke badalAgi baruttade.
18. vastu, viShaya modalAdavugaLannu hesarisuva nAmapadagaLige I
19. pratyayavannu sErisi avakke sambandhisiruva vyaktigaLannu hesarisalu sAdhya
20. vide. idu I pratyayakkiruva modalaneya baLake. udA:
22. adhikAra adhikAri jIva jIvi

aparAdha aparAdhi prANa prANi
viraha virahi rOga rOgi
vyApAra vyApAri dAna dAni

antaha vyaktigaLa guNadharmavannu hesarisalu sAdhyavide. idu I
pratyayakkiruva eraDaneya baLake. udA:

I eraDaneya baLakeyalli baruva nAmapadagaLallella koneya
vyanjanavAgi takAra bandiruvudannu gamanisabahudu. hAgAgi I
nAmapadagaLalli vyaktigaLannu gurutisuvavugaLu ta emba pratyaya
dondigU mattu vyaktigaLa guNadharmavannu gurutisuvavugaLu ti emba
pratyayadondigU baruvuvendU kUDa hELalu sAdhyavide. idE
rItiyalli idakke hinde koTTiruva nAmapadagaLalli vyakti, vastu
modalAduvannu gurutisuvavugaLu a emba pratyayadondigU mattu
antaha vyakti, vastu modalAduvakke sambandhisidavarannu gurutisu
vavugaLu i emba pratyayadondigU baruvuvendU kUDa hELalu
sAdhyavide.

## (೩) ya pratyaya

I pratyayakkU eraDu prAmukhyavAda baLakegaLive. hesarisuva nAma
padagaLige I pratyayavannu sErisi, avugaLige sambandhisiruva vastu,
viShaya illavE guNadharmavannu hesarisuva nAmapadavannu tayArisu
vudu I pratyayada modalaneya baLake. udA:

## (A) ika pratyaya

vudakkAgi kannaDadalli baLakeyAguttade. Adare, kelavu nAmapadagaLu
mAtra I pratyaya sEridAgalU nAmapadagaLAgiyE uLidukoLLuttave.
(samskxtadalli I pratyayada mUlaka tayArAguva padagaLellavU nAma
padagaLE embudannu bEre hELabEkAgillavaShTe!)

vondannu antaha nAmapadagaLige I pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisida

## (೩) u, U mattu av emba svaragaLu av endAguvudu

nAmapada illavE guNapadagaLa modalaneya akSharadalliruva u, U
mattu O emba svaragaLu A padagaLondige ya illavE ika emba
pratyaya sEridAga aniyamitavAgi av emba svaravAgi badalAguttave.
udA:

ya pratyaya ika pratyaya
udAra avdArya purANa pavrANika
sukha savkhya mukha mavkhika
mUla mavlya pUrvAhna pUrvAhnika
sOma savmya lOka lavkika
dUta davtya dEva dayvika

I badalAvaNegaLU aniyamita embudakke pUje-pUjya mattu
pUrva-pUrvika embavugaLannu udAharaNegaLannAgi koDabahudu.

## ೮.೫ kriyApadagaLu

mEleyE sUcisiruvante, samskxtadinda kriyApadagaLu nEravAgi
kannaDakke eravalAgi baruvudilla. idakke badalAgi, avugaLinda tayArAda
nAmapadagaLige kannaDada isu emba pratyayavannu nEravAgi sErisi
illavE avugaLa koneyalli kANisuva pratyayada badalu I pratyaya
vannu baLasi, kriyApadagaLannu tayArisabEkAguttade.

udAharaNegAgi, ane illavE aNe emba pratyayadalli kone
goLLuva halavu nAmapadagaLu A pratyayada badalu isu emba
pratyayadalli konegonDAga nAmapadagaLAgi kANisikoLLuttave. udA:

I eraDu rItiya pratyayagaLalli nakAra elli baruttade mattu
NakAra elli baruttade embudakke samskxtadalli niScitavAda niyamavide.
Adare I niyama kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLalli aShTondu
niScitavAgi uLidilla. sAmAnyavAgi pratyayada eDagaDege rakAra illavE
ShakAra bandideyAdare pratyayadalli nakArada badalu NakAra baruttade
embudAgi kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLalli ondu niyama
illavE olavannu kANalu sAdhyavide. Adare mannaNe mattu prakaTaNe
embavugaLalli kANisuva NakAra I niyamakke apavAdavAgaballudu.

eravalAgi banda nAmapadagaLige nEravAgi isu emba pratyayavannu
sErisuvudara mUlaka kriyApadagaLannu tayArisuvalli eraDu vidhAna
gaLive. A padagaLa koneya akSharada hindina akSharadalli (endare avugaLa
upAntAkSharadalli) uddasvaraviddalli adannu giDDasvaravannAgi mADi
anantara isu pratyayavannu sErisuvudu ondu vidhAna; mattu antaha
yAva badalAvaNeyannU mADade nEravAgi isu pratyayavannu sErisu
vudu innondu vidhAna. udA:

<a id="sec-8-6"></a>

[ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#sec-8-6)

## ೮.೬ jODupadagaLu

kannaDakke samskxtadinda halavAru jODupadagaLU eravalAgi bandive.
mEle (೮.೨)ralli sUcisiruvante, I padagaLa oLaracaneyannu kannaDa
dalli ivugaLa angagaLAgi baruva padagaLige entaha baLakegaLive
embudara AdhArada mEle hELabEkallade, samskxta vyAkaraNagaLalli
ivakke entaha oLaracaneyannu kalpisikoDalAgide embudara AdhArada
mEle hELuvudu sariyalla.

I kAraNakkAgi kannaDadalli kANisuva kelavu eravalAgi banda pada
gaLu samskxtadalli jODupadagaLAgiveyAdarU (kannaDadalli avugaLa
angagaLu svatantra illavE asvatantra padagaLAgi baLakeyallillavAdare)
avannu jODupadagaLendu kareyade oLaracaneyillada padagaLendE
kareyabEkAguttade.

oLaracaneyannu kalpisikoLLalu sAdhyaviruvantaha eravalAgi banda
padagaLu kannaDadalli prAmukhyavAgi eraDu vargagaLalli kANisuttave.
modalaneya anga nAmapadavAgiruvavugaLu mattu modalaneya anga
guNapadavAgiruvavugaLu embudAgi mEle (೨.೬.೫)ralli kannaDada
jODupadagaLannu hesarisida hAgeyE ivannU hesarisalu sAdhyavide.

ivugaLalli modalaneya anga nAmapadavAgiruva jODupadagaLu
avugaLa eraDu angagaLannu sambandhaka pratyayada mUlaka jODisidavu
gaLAgiruttave, mattu modalaneya anga guNapadavAgiruva jODupada
gaLu antaha guNapadavannu nAmapadada eDakke nillisi tayArisidavugaLA
giruttave. udA:

## (೧) modalaneya anga nAmapadavAgiruva jODupadagaLu

mAnahAni mAnada hAni
mUrtipUje mUrtiya pUje
lagnapatrike lagnada patrike
vidyAbhyAsa vidyeya abhyAsa

## (೨) modalaneya anga guNapadavAgiruva jODupadagaLu

I jODupadagaLalli kelavakke Ada emba kriyArUpavannu baLasi vigraha
vAkyavannu hELalu sAdhyavide (udA: dxDhavAda manassu, gADhavAda
nidre). Adare intaha oLaracaneyallU modalaneya angavAgi ondu
guNapadavE kANisikoLLuttade. adu vigrahavAkyadalli nEravAgi
nAmapada deduru baruva badalu AkhyAtada sthAnadalli bandide, aShTe.

eraDakkinta jAsti padagaLinda tayArAgiruva jODupadagaLa baLake
kannaDadalli bahaLa aparUpa. Adare samskxtadalli intaha jODupada
gaLu hEraLavAgiddu, avugaLalli kelavu kannaDakkU eravalAgi bandive.
ivu sAmAnyavAgi eraDeraDu padagaLannu sErisuvantaha eraDu athavA
jAsti staragaLalli tayArAguttave.

udAharaNegAgi, ariShaDvarga emba padavannu pariSIlisabahudu.
modalaneya staradalli ShaT 'Aru' mattu varga 'gumpu' emberaDu
padagaLannu sErisi ShaDvarga emba padavannu tayArisi, anantara
eraDaneya staradalli A padakke ari 'Satru' emba padavannu sErisi I
padavannu tayArisalAgideyendu hELalu sAdhyavide.




idE rItiyalli kuSAgramati emba padavannu modalige kuSAgra
emba padavannu tayArisi, anantara eraDaneya staradalli adakke mati
emba padavannu sErisuvudara mUlaka tayArisalAgideyendu hELalu
sAdhyavide.

## a.೭ sArAmSa

kannaDakke samskxtadinda eravalAgi bandiruva padagaLannu kannaDada
vyAkaraNagaLalli sAmAnyavAgi avakke samskxta vyAkaraNagaLalli koTTiruva
oLaracanegaLannE koTTu vivarisuvudu rUDhi. Adare idu sariyalla. I
padagaLige kannaDadalli kannaDadavE Ada oLaracanegaLive.

samskxtadalli pUrvapratyayaviruva padagaLu kannaDadalli jODu
padagaLAgi kANisikoLLabahudu, illavE pratyayaviruvavugaLAgi kANisi
koLLabahudu. parapratyayaviruva padagaLannu samskxtadalli kxt mattu
taddita pratyayaviruvavugaLendu vingaDisuvudu rUDhi. Adare kannaDada
maTTige I vingaDaNegintalU nAmapada illavE guNapadakke bEre bEre
rItiya pratyayagaLannu sErisi nAmapadavannu tayArisalAgideyE
athavA guNapadavannu tayArisalAgideyE emba viShayada AdhArada
mEle I padagaLannu varNisuvudE heccu upayuktavAda vidhAna.

jODupadagaLannu samskxtadalli prAmukhyavAgi avugaLa angagaLAgi
bandiruva padagaLalli pradhAna pada yAvudu (endare, kEndra bindu
yAva angada mEle bILuttade) emba viShayada AdhArada mEle,
tatpuruSha, bahuvrIhi, avyayIbhAva, dvandva modalAda samAsagaLAgi
vingaDisuvudu rUDhi. Adare, kannaDakke eravalAgi bandiruva samskxtada
jODupadagaLannu I rIti vingaDisuva badalu, avugaLa modalaneya
angavAgi bandiruva pada nAmapadavE athavA guNapadavE emba
viShayada AdhArada mEle vingaDisuvudE heccu txptikaravAda vidhAna.




<a id="adhyAya-9"></a>

[English →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-en#chapter-9--conclusion) | [ಕನ್ನಡ →](./03-kannaDa-padagaLa-oLaracane-kn#adhyAya-9)

## adhyAya ombattu
muktAya

pratiyondu bhAShegU adaradE Ada vyAkaraNa parampareyondu
beLedu baruva avaSyakateyide. illavAdare adara vyAkaraNada mEle
bareda barahagaLu A bhASheya mUlasUtragaLannu pratibimbisuva badalu
bEre bhASheya mUlasUtragaLannu adara mEle hEruvantAguttade.
intaha mUlasUtragaLu bErondu bhAShAkuTumbakke sEriruva bhAShe
yavAgiddare avugaLindAguva tondare innaShTu heccinadu.

kannaDa vyAkaraNada mEle bareda barahagaLalli heccinavU intaha
tondarege silukikonDive. avu prAmukhyavAgi samskxta bhASheya
vyAkaraNa parampareyinda prabhAvitavAgiruvudE idakke kAraNa. samskxta
bhAShe inDO-Aryan emba bhAShAkuTumbakke sEriruva bhAShe,
mattu kannaDa idakkinta tIra bhinnavAgiruva drAviDa bhAShAkuTumbakke
sEriruva bhAShe. I eraDu bhAShegaLa vyAkaraNagaLu bahaLa maTTige
ondarinda ondu bhinnavAgiruvuvAda kAraNa, samskxtada vyAkaraNa
parampareyalli barediruva I barahagaLella kannaDa vyAkaraNada nijasvarUpa
vannu tiLisi hELuvalli bahaLa maTTige asamarthavAgive.

I pustakadalli nAnu prayatnisiruva kannaDa padagaLa oLaracaneya
pariSIlane, adarallU kannaDadalli baruva jODupadagaLa oLaracaneya
pariSIlane, I viShayavannu spaShTamADikoTTide. samskxtakkU kannaDakkU
naDuviruva vyatyAsagaLalli padavargagaLige sambandhisida vyatyAsa bahaLa
prAmukhyavAdudu. kannaDadalli nAmapada, kriyApada mattu guNapada
gaLemba mUru mukhya padavargagaLive; Adare samskxtadalli nAmapada
mattu kriyApadagaLemba eraDE eraDu mukhya padavargagaLu mAtra
ive. kannaDada padagaLannu samskxtakke anuvAdisuvAga, adaralliruva



guNapadagaLalli heccinavannU nAmapadagaLAgiyE anuvAdisabEkAguttade
embudarinda I viShaya spaShTavAguttade.

I prAmukhyavAda vyatyAsada pariNAmavannu I eraDu bhAShegaLalli
kANisuva padagaLa oLaracaneyalli bahaLa spaShTavAgi kANabahudu. udA
haraNegAgi, samskxtadalli baruva jODupadagaLalli heccinavU eraDu
(athavA jAsti) nAmapadagaLannu oTTu sErisi tayArisidantahavugaLu.
Adare kannaDadalli nAmapadagaLondige bEre nAmapadagaLannu mAtra
vallade kriyApada mattu guNapadagaLannu sErisiyU jODupadagaLannu
tayArisalu sAdhyavide. I kAraNakkAgi padavargagaLa AdhArada mEle
tayArisida jODupadagaLa vibhajane samskxtada maTTige aShTondu
prAmukhyavendu tOruvudillavAdarU kannaDada maTTige idu atyanta
prAmukhyavAda vibhajane.

samskxtadalli jODupadagaLannu padagucchagaLinda bErpaDisalu hecci
neDegaLallU avugaLa angagaLAgi bandiruva nAmapadagaLalli koneya
dannu biTTu itara nAmapadagaLondige) linga-vacana-vibhaktigaLannu
sUcisuva pratyaya bandideyE athavA illavE emba viShayavannu
AdhAravAgi irisikoLLalu sAdhyavide. Adare kannaDadalli idu heccineDe
gaLallU sAdhyavAgadu. guNapadagaLu kannaDada padagucchagaLalli nEravAgi
(endare pratyayagaLa sahAyavillade) nAmapadagaLondige baruvuvAda
kAraNa, antaha padagucchagaLannu jODupadagaLinda bErpaDisalu
bEreyE vidhAnagaLannu baLasabEkAguttade. kannaDa mattu samskxtagaLa
naDuviruva I vyatyAsavannu gamanisada kannaDada vayyAkaraNigaLu
kannaDada padagucchagaLalli halavannu jODupadagaLendu kareyahOgi
gondalakkeDemADiddAre (೫.೬.೫ nODi).

samskxtadalli baruva oLaracaneyillada padagaLellavU kriyAdhAtu
gaLE. adaralli baruva nAmapadagaLalli heccinavannU intaha kriyA
dhAtugaLige bEre bEre rItiya pratyayagaLannu sErisuvudara mUlaka
tayArisabEkAguttade. hAgAgi, samskxtadalli baruva pratyayagaLannu
kxt‌pratyaya (endare kriyAdhAtuvinondige nEravAgi sEruva pratyaya)
mattu taddita pratyaya (endare hAge sEruvudara mUlaka tayArA
giruva padagaLondige baruva pratyaya) embudAgi eraDu vargagaLalli
vingaDisuvudara mUlaka adara padagaLa oLaracaneyannu spaShTavAgi
vivarisalu sAdhyavAguttade.




Adare kannaDadalli kriyAdhAtu, nAmadhAtu mattu guNadhAtu
embudAgi mUru bEre bEre rItiya dhAtugaLiddu, avu mUrakkU
bEre bEre rItiya pratyayagaLannu sErisuvudara mUlaka kriyApada,
nAmapada mattu guNapadagaLannu tayArisalu sAdhyavide. hIge tayA
risuvAga ondu vargada dhAtuvininda innondu vargada padavannU
(udA: kriyAdhAtuvininda nAmapadavannu illavE guNadhAtuvininda
kriyApadavannu) paDeyalu sAdhyavide. hAgAgi, kannaDada pratyayagaLannu
samskxtada pratyayagaLa hAge kxt mattu taddita emba eraDu varga
gaLalli vibhajisuvudu adara padagaLa oLaracaneya varNanege aShTondu
upayuktavAguva vibhajaneyalla.

samskxtada vyAkaraNa parampareya hAgeyE lyATin mattu
ingliSh bhASheya vyAkaraNa paramparegaLU A bhAShegaLa vyAkaraNagaLannu
varNisu valli upayOgakke baraballallade kannaDada vyAkaraNavannu
varNisuvalli heccige prayOjanakke baralAravu. kannaDa vyAkaraNadalli
adaradE Ada halavAru vaySiShTyagaLiddu, avannu kanDukoLLalu
adaradE Ada vyAkaraNa parampareyondannu beLesikoLLuva
avaSyakateyide.

manuShyaru prANigaLinda bhinnavAda vyaktigaLAgi vikAsagonDAga
avarondige avara bhASheyU vikAsagonDirabEku; mattu manuShyaru
anantara bEre bEre samAjagaLAgi vibhajitarAdAga idarondige
avarADuva bhASheyU bEre bEre bhAShegaLAgi vibhajitavAgirabEku.
hAgAgi, manuShyaroLagella hEge sAmyavideyO hAgeyE avarADuva
bhAShegaLa naDuveyU sAmyaviddE irabEku. I kAraNakkAgi, kannaDa,
samskxta, lyATin, ingliSh mAtravallade jagattinalliruva itara
sAvirAru bhAShegaLa naDuveyU bEre bEre rItiya sAmyagaLannu
kANalu sAdhyavide. intaha sAmyagaLa AdhArada mEle I ellA
sAvirAru bhAShegaLigU anvayisuvantaha vyAkaraNa parampareyondannu
kalpisikoLLalu sAdhyavide. intaha vyAkaraNa parampareyannu kalpisikoLLuva
prayatna Iga halavu daSakagaLindalU naDeyuttA ide.

Adare I bhAShegaLoLage sAmya mAtravallade vyatyAsavU ideyAda
kAraNa, avugaLa naDuviruva sAmyavannu pratinidhIkarisuva vyAkaraNa
parampare mAtravallade vyatyAsavannu tOrisikoDuva vyAkaraNa parampare
yU atyavaSya. kannaDada maTTige I eraDanE rItiya vyAkaraNa
parampareyinnU siddhavAgilla. adakkAgi nAvu heccina gamana koDuva




avaSyakateyideyembudE I pustakavannu bareyuvudarallidda mUla
uddESa.
